---
title: Algebruh's 2nd
---
*Organized in order to balance saves with difficulty and memorization needed. Leans rather heavily toward memorization.*  
# Notes
This document is organized in order to minimize the difficulty of memorizing/learning 2nd, while still trying to keep the reliability and usefulness of setups. Due to my biases, it favors memorization and learning of new setups more than simplification.  
PCs are organized based on JL parity and whether or not it has T.  
Sometimes, I saves will be included due to the difficulty of achieving 100% O/T not being practical.
- Asterisks have been added to denote when I saves are included or necessary.
- “-extra” means that that header has setups that are not necessary for the original method
- “-alt” means that it is an entirely different method, commonly one that is differently tailored.
- “(T/I)” means that the method focuses on T and I saving, unlike most methods which focus on T and O saving.
# Even JL, no T
These PCs are incredibly good at saving T, mostly due to their bag composition lending itself to that very nicely. The main problem comes with how simple you can make the setups. 
## IJLO 
IJLO is undoubtedly the best 2nd PC out there, with next to no contest. If it really drives the point home, the easiest method that I would recommend for IJLO is the 100% save T method. It’s a total of essentially four solves.  
Notably, you can also take a number of two-line PCs on this. The most common, with 28.57% cover, is simply a 2L into no-O 6th, which is relatively good. I’d advise against doing this if you’re going for long runs, as it leads very quickly back into first PC.  
If you’re looking for a slightly different method, and you don’t like those extra solves, there’s this six-solve method that’s based off of the original 100% T method.  
![](https://lh7-rt.googleusercontent.com/docsz/AD_4nXdkBmRCT_snhT-OubIMpMAE2vLYo27_V8_SGyGiT7rSQrbsGtpLmLd5MGCq-KnKvBLqaYIAcQ4ujMlYYMih5yCZTTNe_YNpq77vPOnS7BJpLKNH92K8PE8yZHpZy3vGpXWtVO1hHFaxysYvOSVW2PMw1aIP?key=rxGnIOzTXwvvF_Z1hOaPWA)![](https://lh7-rt.googleusercontent.com/docsz/AD_4nXeHmIaxl-vH13S_WpA9eSpSww1hLqpDeiBjVtn6sskWwWHRmP2xBKb4S3u_XPaScpf7jfmN9eGr6AvX-oNU183oO9PsbqYjQvD1h2SJkyAOhm-vgXtd5dFBxFAE4BTkBhcfFqyDPzLolvuV228ZN6LtGiZD?key=rxGnIOzTXwvvF_Z1hOaPWA)![](https://lh7-rt.googleusercontent.com/docsz/AD_4nXeUjBbFaMB8g79AHlUdq6MAi5xupJjgjdtL6gXAgHsFhbR_D5ETS6mO0xEEnbCFRRY4AB8JKCeyTFC4TL94Z0ex_QA6CizrT_tmYTzI2XPF4uR-WLeo79p1NNCnP74e9B4nJD_dVgzreKxGWkSgXORmxkY?key=rxGnIOzTXwvvF_Z1hOaPWA)

These are the S and Z queue-based setups. They both save T, and fail to be built on \[TJ]!,S or \[TL]!,Z queues, respectively. You’ll be able to use the next set of setups if you can’t build these, or for queues like \[TIL]! and \[TLO]! which sometimes have to use the larger set of solves for Sandbox.  
![](https://lh7-rt.googleusercontent.com/docsz/AD_4nXcZ2BSbCbfug34wjFvdkESLvVQIQOkU680eOqEtJG6shCi2q4yO7l6iGGQWgSizZMtBkJ2bOsnI8dNvXWWFeJ9Vi65rzvpX2EGHSXfkG37VT-TTARdRhAWH-5fzLgUvObVy4c9qgdE6G-C_sVqOZjzuiePb?key=rxGnIOzTXwvvF_Z1hOaPWA)![](https://lh7-rt.googleusercontent.com/docsz/AD_4nXdhbQooTjKNgwrgMnbcCfbeqd3XHIeJBJMC_ToxO3fnuFEe4oFrQEgflGPnvOain_uwscvzfcdPJylgqvB4UnlQVbwkd7uiOVk59VQShQSnG_MsbWx8gUPlqULh-6-6jO62IeTkUKUt9Qhbgwc2XGEfB19o?key=rxGnIOzTXwvvF_Z1hOaPWA)![](https://lh7-rt.googleusercontent.com/docsz/AD_4nXdXFCyj6N1BungNWnRjfqTIYa5eiUb7JCuC0Y9yGIhfSdHOsvrhyJoKpbdP6fYHnzscFW_sVqxDAN-hzdaAQ9TpNsV4aIScSADLaLmCftxXPSzV5qqOvRt2nU0dpvarw5dL5g8sx3YhiVmRvOJ3AvBvA_Bl?key=rxGnIOzTXwvvF_Z1hOaPWA)

These both save O, and in combination with the S and Z queue-based setups, entirely mitigate all of the weird-solve queues for the 100% T method, including one of the normal solves, knocking it down to just two. The “sandbox” setup can even be extended to it’s 4-piece form.  
![](https://lh7-rt.googleusercontent.com/docsz/AD_4nXckaxKsUfV7ms79aW_pNefuUsiRhOGp1K3bxD3mBXqKVGhDajJhD0rcyDQcTpZCigecHGFZlLfYlToXqv6H77hLbdo0NdDS1hdqot_MjS3I8zzOGAd3DYeqXnNNK7fOG6ChuUb8dOvFN_3K-DqPFcnSDfsi?key=rxGnIOzTXwvvF_Z1hOaPWA)![](https://lh7-rt.googleusercontent.com/docsz/AD_4nXcwxtDnT_tL-Mhs2_adOgnzY4GUZy1FrA19PzZLnPzQ9KWiXw1vjqCHOdsDoAXTb1kOO8heZyxs4p7dv5KWqJAXg2iEkM_REQMECuV1DocbkkTXq4144EaYcmn3k2zHeMvFaTtNVsI_s-mOws4XP1giyaPm?key=rxGnIOzTXwvvF_Z1hOaPWA)![](https://lh7-rt.googleusercontent.com/docsz/AD_4nXct1gH9rBs3vj1G27PeN3wR4Cb1QItbCBfA1XpWj2hJuFtSw_TcqS6YJwL1SKpGDZawXnHXhQnnKYlDUHkHkTpNz6b5qQdA7b1TcGK7vpF08qzyJO5K-8UF_akt38YB5H16075__LL6leSuU8rocwIvHNJh?key=rxGnIOzTXwvvF_Z1hOaPWA)
The solves are based on SZ order. Watch out for weird skims and 180 spins.  
## IJLO (T)
This is a method for getting 100% T out of IJLO 2nd with the easiest way possible.  
![](https://lh7-rt.googleusercontent.com/docsz/AD_4nXdkBmRCT_snhT-OubIMpMAE2vLYo27_V8_SGyGiT7rSQrbsGtpLmLd5MGCq-KnKvBLqaYIAcQ4ujMlYYMih5yCZTTNe_YNpq77vPOnS7BJpLKNH92K8PE8yZHpZy3vGpXWtVO1hHFaxysYvOSVW2PMw1aIP?key=rxGnIOzTXwvvF_Z1hOaPWA)![](https://lh7-rt.googleusercontent.com/docsz/AD_4nXeHmIaxl-vH13S_WpA9eSpSww1hLqpDeiBjVtn6sskWwWHRmP2xBKb4S3u_XPaScpf7jfmN9eGr6AvX-oNU183oO9PsbqYjQvD1h2SJkyAOhm-vgXtd5dFBxFAE4BTkBhcfFqyDPzLolvuV228ZN6LtGiZD?key=rxGnIOzTXwvvF_Z1hOaPWA)![](https://lh7-rt.googleusercontent.com/docsz/AD_4nXeUjBbFaMB8g79AHlUdq6MAi5xupJjgjdtL6gXAgHsFhbR_D5ETS6mO0xEEnbCFRRY4AB8JKCeyTFC4TL94Z0ex_QA6CizrT_tmYTzI2XPF4uR-WLeo79p1NNCnP74e9B4nJD_dVgzreKxGWkSgXORmxkY?key=rxGnIOzTXwvvF_Z1hOaPWA)  
![](https://lh7-rt.googleusercontent.com/docsz/AD_4nXdZVsdr8_WtudRZA6YZoFKddKNc1DcvOPotwQjfpRQi2vcFbpLviWgK00fYPCl7zSgH001d7YBdW5262qkRCYxBqKfxEor27GeTiNyq1bTTupDyx7qdKIqzUtVfO22n4MV1uPpZ5QE3vUNUwEfg798IP6H7?key=rxGnIOzTXwvvF_Z1hOaPWA)![](https://lh7-rt.googleusercontent.com/docsz/AD_4nXcRQeOed7Dx3zb-zhhguyba1RIQ27zLLj7-IZtf9CrHHt_HV5m7FiNQKseGfsYMB0molyewWgRe2hNujBGJRmvCHKF6kYzw7AdfP_jzhPj_hjd6yR9lhXtWN22XbqTZo82I6x0qNLnC4L3gunAChPHifXET?key=rxGnIOzTXwvvF_Z1hOaPWA)![](https://lh7-rt.googleusercontent.com/docsz/AD_4nXdoPlsTH_HSwME6n7zr2RYloHsUDBTu42sZtXJrpv7TwMF0KF61WcHZQWhB6F2jd324RnIicHLk-7nk7vL0irbFgyPWC3yXd0emVr13OOxXAp3Rtx5V-cJj1dC5R91UHlb0ZpD7MlqJWhOSgxmBApLdP5ZS?key=rxGnIOzTXwvvF_Z1hOaPWA)  
First, we can borrow the S and Z queue-based setups. Note that they’re specifically for S before J and Z before L.  
If we see J before S or L before Z, we can do a partial version of the four-piece sandbox setup, which also works if we don’t see any of JLSZ. ([TIO]! queues) Build the setup that holds L when you see L, build the setup that holds J when you see J.
![](https://lh7-rt.googleusercontent.com/docsz/AD_4nXdTBtn71NtQqS-l25wU35Q7mjbnRBEw7QbzpJmbLzctezpiSUrOENwjgGGRvvOL4Bkh14kd59-B8GvW4vJQxTXgkrdiaQlbygQKY_R2NliZchI7gpXdIk97SqEI-ykoMqCZU9C886S9cusbXGaTu77sSeL8?key=rxGnIOzTXwvvF_Z1hOaPWA)  
![](https://lh7-rt.googleusercontent.com/docsz/AD_4nXeueHHg4EWSdUxSwjbiWzJDV-mB86z32dG0KQ-m44QK5FRP1Ag08uw9idT7hynB8HySY9zW-cmHXVPOk2weRjIXg_NriEq785ZBaTCIiVloc5m0Qks1xU42Gloh9HsruyQgqUvWVnYdWiF8irtKepCwCsxa?key=rxGnIOzTXwvvF_Z1hOaPWA)![](https://lh7-rt.googleusercontent.com/docsz/AD_4nXcgUUgsf15XosyDTWqSvnAw6AFD87vSwTqNOUK5zYHXrLY-0_Fg9BbHeFWQZxrUhkqunD8aIse3MNo8X6TSp0rnZqORPxTyBIM69nqyCXIPtNRYM7trb6WAEwCzicSG7gSv6YrZ7Md3uS1x43hT8qgOf1bg?key=rxGnIOzTXwvvF_Z1hOaPWA)![](https://lh7-rt.googleusercontent.com/docsz/AD_4nXdQ8U9UBiDUpU5C3Olp5e4J7eTn7X8x2yqTmwYHnrEPg5bupQGSa2v09yH0SMiIE0uBMeGcTEnUdMvSqxhHXN-TiHIvEqoWboHLFEFBWsF9Q8QINDe0uQpV3IcjoKgTi7_yyVtjZ_4_Y_78JNWwcK6WxnNb?key=rxGnIOzTXwvvF_Z1hOaPWA)  
The solves are: S before Z, JZ before S, and Z<S<J. If you use them in the order presented here, it becomes: S before Z, S last, J last.  
If you see TIO, then all of the out-of-order placements will work, and you can place down the L to use the first two solves.  
## IJLS/IJLZ
IJLS/Z is also incredibly good, but it lacks the simplicity part that IJLO exceeds expectations in. The best setup that I could successfully find is this 3 piece 100% T/O setup that has ten solves. Seven save T, and three save O.  It also does have a single one-piece queue-based setup, for Z.  
![](https://lh7-rt.googleusercontent.com/docsz/AD_4nXeYy60Bu6oSG-inwAM2xe3_3MpHOMq8N2SEWM64u61TC_2kGVm7TyTU3Pdyo5TCAEd0ZACpnUJqKg9Q_ekP76L-S9DT8DumIGHmJAvrPbnO8yJtAAOZGOU_kUSw-2cFgcRc3wucPeViuFC65uTkXs3krw8?key=rxGnIOzTXwvvF_Z1hOaPWA)![](https://lh7-rt.googleusercontent.com/docsz/AD_4nXfLN4jRiqwNBJEDr2VQdKlfDfLutPmuIhLxD4gcD9AGSRRcKSMYvucbkdpfgrkibUvR9RPf9gbQV20RBOHAsFOx6UXifTEs_4lIWiRI8pcFM6azsXMqPq4xcJch_UGwUxNuejE_ZD6z916je5l8e4HofuSZ?key=rxGnIOzTXwvvF_Z1hOaPWA)![](https://lh7-rt.googleusercontent.com/docsz/AD_4nXfmvozaHwCTJOwQO8T5ITlkT5qpUdhEjZ65AqPbuFqTewzEqurJdfzGomAIIbr8XJzF6Z78DspIOcoaOkbhgFvvQC8VpOHZvqQAaXEWwHZDxrSVWAyon55hr-J4BPGyS-1fZnp2ZC3PqBalLEYw740XPOVf?key=rxGnIOzTXwvvF_Z1hOaPWA)![](https://lh7-rt.googleusercontent.com/docsz/AD_4nXeNwhbIDkR5TOmtjLQryLNvS52LCp4vopmEh-UFL_I6JBe2I2AcqFdVGd6kY1vN-nQwFBQ3YHKtvUlIXDC04ZF5GLgyeNGvdkehlECDQKL7XLkGMKM3g_jhTh2d0yHIZQNXUzKTlcsYICIwSe_VQb87jQ4W?key=rxGnIOzTXwvvF_Z1hOaPWA)  
It saves T, and fails to be built on \[ST]!,Z queues.  
![](https://lh7-rt.googleusercontent.com/docsz/AD_4nXfe1hRmDNZo0jBIWRn9qZtetWpL9-qKcoXXzDAQJ-PwNl83HTTfLi10U6IKRsPXYPBXxaU-a7FCOEEKqlB0BNXWRLbs0AVi9YeYSEPEyXtBMFzATAfnrxW8z3Xarso1fGgL5syEVqVWmiYI8iDkFFphxYs?key=rxGnIOzTXwvvF_Z1hOaPWA)

## IJLS/IJLZ-alt
Again, this is my personal method. This one isn’t specifically personal preference, but it focuses on more strict decision-making rather than just “here’s a setup, go wild”. I died on IJLZ 2nd once, near a PB, which prompted me to actually go out and make a method I’d like.
![](https://lh7-rt.googleusercontent.com/docsz/AD_4nXdmT8jDlgSxuVgNsK64ZzaTFhjoW2uezdG5hQCsoOd9kbbb8BQRGSFnke7fPatSJdMB60SXWwP1tuGNgLlaBjM0Jt6wctfnIox8E9Hwm6J4k01nzFB1IYH-I-Oono_1RLrKwxxAyl6UriYMzT-aAwDVDXAy?key=rxGnIOzTXwvvF_Z1hOaPWA)![](https://lh7-rt.googleusercontent.com/docsz/AD_4nXeqoeJtHu59ftXhlzcncloKAESRBr1YIR57mEi9TCSErvxUV-h9WypBbPKsYcdFGTRNNiMcAuxgGI3LYZ4Jr80M4N63ynhRdgOKW1eq5hgWQ9k_LArePpEfmxMXE_QAvrk3v0u28yMDoR0TFU0AeRe_LOi3?key=rxGnIOzTXwvvF_Z1hOaPWA)![](https://lh7-rt.googleusercontent.com/docsz/AD_4nXfJJeNmghn2FJAaAvuAnij1q73iWKbch9kVEN7HTDp5yxQLwE2xBPs58CySYFjJaMSomvdSI7uTZxZ154mliLU3MVRYxVr-Qq8jNgvMFT6JghFXSP4Qcok1msY1ywze9h9aqAT7ufQL4MrqjaeVSQEje4IS?key=rxGnIOzTXwvvF_Z1hOaPWA)  
See S before Z queue-based setup. Fails to be built on \[ST]!,Z queues. When I first published this method, I actually forgot to cover those specific queues.

## JLOS/JLOZ*
JLOS and JLOZ suffer even more compared to IJLS on the front of balancing good saves with simplicity. I’m using a mix of queue-based setups and “fallback” setups for this.

![](https://lh7-rt.googleusercontent.com/docsz/AD_4nXf-ZEzMnL0X2DBRF1g8K6t2FCkqGSMLiifOBjl0rRp8VKcpJ1KURc8clIVqlA1ROijRCHktJSywOSBKsM1t23e9POrOXLhVeUEHFXKrbAZb2Gwf9CZgoZ4ktm0QFWePoShkDJaW3wqKFnUMkHyV5P_gpzm_?key=rxGnIOzTXwvvF_Z1hOaPWA)![](https://lh7-rt.googleusercontent.com/docsz/AD_4nXcA111egOZwJRVcXDLmnZvctnctxT8va92GZkxfRQ3Y_ABbXCeEamoHgJCbyuPZVC5xhRnD6Z-e9LNLiqqoDljllUNrnlxdQxrkyMSjLRpF-bRfB6q0hCsDVpCnNR--CIWYqK6aFu17qFFsC5PCONf1CdX5?key=rxGnIOzTXwvvF_Z1hOaPWA)![](https://lh7-rt.googleusercontent.com/docsz/AD_4nXfJV9Fgd9gnwbJ52nRi3tOCd3fEexcpr1M92IXhInjZVvWTQW8posg9EooU0sVAdD8_Shs5tUjSaYgm7vjikFT-r8JYiQeTDXu9W1CtWs-WfG0AGI_x0FMfezl8X4LT0HEHQNlEx9xhiuD6cOXN59K5r0-S?key=rxGnIOzTXwvvF_Z1hOaPWA)

That last solve is specifically for \[TIO]! queues where J is revealed directly after. It’s the only save I solve included.
## JLOS/JLOZ-alt
This is a method with more of what I call “faulty one-piece QBs”. They work mostly, but can catch you off guard if you use them incorrectly. The JLOS method is so old here that you can see the old color for gray minos.
![](https://lh7-rt.googleusercontent.com/docsz/AD_4nXcBg4amiLu3Uh93V2SacQZw0Uu9MZHgWxs7xL0b26kTBZbh1xVp5fMNIa_hF7hi-pg5eC_80igr8gTdiAfqbOPjF3_ehT7DWm3XCMlcL6YhWKtqkd61SePjaWoPa9jRo9iL-pF5u5IKGKAlDYGItH2R8JkI?key=rxGnIOzTXwvvF_Z1hOaPWA)![](https://lh7-rt.googleusercontent.com/docsz/AD_4nXfBWpbm8SCK1OJDBcPvPJ9vsZz9PTqHnafSZtTKXfNjhJKg3HT9r246AWLiN2k9ujAj7tM141MAfi16ajkLBgoN7i-DJo9vLWWNfP1Qd2sYTNUbnMhZsjQSpHe3-u3S816VBxM_SeIW5B-zQJCgVFvvRe5x?key=rxGnIOzTXwvvF_Z1hOaPWA)![](https://lh7-rt.googleusercontent.com/docsz/AD_4nXf7XT1gjEFASowti6QdEVUFPT_YNjTNOMgQuReUzmHQcGjoFdpKhplPJDEIi2pvUZHtRkCjR8uro_pVrR9nWIt7PcfLDxfkv_aQJJWT0fCTJ96IO4wCYVtR5I6Jt-lzJV6MjgXuatkFps9ASjPntpSOsPFk?key=rxGnIOzTXwvvF_Z1hOaPWA)
![](https://lh7-rt.googleusercontent.com/docsz/AD_4nXdiuej1YLFweda2aJMIxtGN_WoQ21WAZWlNTrZQ3xCBdBOmiY-Sl_xCAX70K1Woz4a9RYACf-QT5XQSI4YcrcggtGP_HDFC0WUv05tx62tJSHRZHvdmwLUmzMqsVml2cRgt2pb9QbGzFd_VbCQmxqsjOs4s?key=rxGnIOzTXwvvF_Z1hOaPWA)![](https://lh7-rt.googleusercontent.com/docsz/AD_4nXeljGuXx-y05gOmVrRvTQ1ls-TpYIrHo_8aWKA3J5ycVhK-k7z7wfo9hqblFFATEVGpr25cfnfoM6Q_oSo2670muhpk7uaN1g5inF3YyB2o_ILOOdxB7FnSl_wfOJLoX9XXmXVO8Kalbcf_3yC3nsdu1zo?key=rxGnIOzTXwvvF_Z1hOaPWA)![](https://lh7-rt.googleusercontent.com/docsz/AD_4nXet081eFMu7kAVV7y2UayTV8fRkikkyXxKjKJjOLUwQmsecf9o6UBTT2JiIIwvgSVMUJS004Y9tdczZxCAAlmYm1emrdKqefmNjzt7lGXb9cwKjsaO32iRbibd4x4Yk8B32d0vpUOstp4NL6sDJFR24Uck?key=rxGnIOzTXwvvF_Z1hOaPWA)  
It starts off with the standard Z queue-based setup and the fallback OZ queue-based setup.

Then, the order gets switched a bit; the JIO queue-based setup comes up here.

Then, there’s the faulty one-piece QB for S, which will be used for any \[ILSO]p3 queue:  
![](https://lh7-rt.googleusercontent.com/docsz/AD_4nXdWNbD8qLUgEHBpm4RZnip-S2FPJamLeWW7lXI1Jv9G1UtMEp8ELNkPO0Sl6JGNrHoTKsHJdo-_fxrxeX4mWxaUnkItsXZX9Obi-WZ4tAv2AMQcXnriRgo2cbOi2-l3VyJ-vFdsKcSY5-W0zeu0_VIflWtY?key=rxGnIOzTXwvvF_Z1hOaPWA)

The first solve covers most queues (any with an L) but for \[IOS]! queues may need to use the second one when the queue has J last and Z before L.

## JLSZ 
One of the nice things about JLSZ (shared with IJLO and IOSZ) is that setups and queue-based setups can be freely mirrored based on the queue. But, JLSZ is a little bit less cooperative and has to rely on the aforementioned mirroring to a very high degree. I’ve simplified the mirroring part to be human-doable.

![](https://lh7-rt.googleusercontent.com/docsz/AD_4nXchubkFnnHqUjRiTYqYdnQgGF_AUIQ1Ks12LpK-Ex5SW2lDl5OKtR-GJesBMQ3NZOXVyQf6WhP5ckwA3M5PuG9Qo1Y9w01MvnwJ2_6ai2LL1FUiLUexKygOJcfRtmLfzxnObcc6aJYgTqSoFWn7bxpSw7c?key=rxGnIOzTXwvvF_Z1hOaPWA)![](https://lh7-rt.googleusercontent.com/docsz/AD_4nXe9UEkypzAEBtSTFTCQCyt1DeET9hd41n8uK4rNxF4jYR_qk6BKk6LW10HbuvmXJNk-UiqwVKlkr-1_3I1hEzNNFboYN1dVST4Wahsub5LoW9acKIDinR1y_ET-iMDYERaILnx0oKiSwzwVY2VWuicAFPyv?key=rxGnIOzTXwvvF_Z1hOaPWA)![](https://lh7-rt.googleusercontent.com/docsz/AD_4nXcgK58-UjWunNZZR-g1j1HFOOFrBv1LB4LUEwNoYhsf8VI6M1GR4SuwI4ij7-DSf-3kR-0Mef-9xOJSjEisZKz8SP1eEsdtMpr2EDc5oeGS2Iddhd_y2VsvdG_fy_ZSexe-402DaRZPu_mrW1agBywihKg?key=rxGnIOzTXwvvF_Z1hOaPWA)  
![](https://lh7-rt.googleusercontent.com/docsz/AD_4nXeS6Udi4EGGKsDioYepWwIxTNvjR1D7OCOAno8pXbXnEnIZEJVXqkT8vQhgpnIYDZsqS2fECOr0Mt7A1xy1_q8pY1CZJOca1tRagXFetsR5OtZTjxGdHSP26XfN_Wt4jOqe2mFOTG31EZFqbVEcbcCrPDs?key=rxGnIOzTXwvvF_Z1hOaPWA)![](https://lh7-rt.googleusercontent.com/docsz/AD_4nXcJpTYRv1OgRcnJyyWmsWjaFhVEiMlxq2cqw6_r4ETDKkG2Q2-fztOvMzyoH8K4f8JCCEANyohqgVz-F4nVz5v1mFX9mNxnKvuKf3_F4VioDQDIZDGqffGGwMyIpUI9pYz2IC2Tx-7NVS-MmfWB1R-bVGRC?key=rxGnIOzTXwvvF_Z1hOaPWA)![](https://lh7-rt.googleusercontent.com/docsz/AD_4nXdSXUeL8svXfziqzcMPdAqF2RtE-ojWBFVUklgAlDkwlxxULw_EaLP94Lxsnit3uCIsbbEBdnx7E9bB7w1zbX1VBSzCklV4n6DzNe4hLRwy4vl1MxL38_zRbxv-JvH5XDHpyf2F6ASYIX0HGAoVlWCoz0I?key=rxGnIOzTXwvvF_Z1hOaPWA)

This one will be used a bit weirdly. It’s going to be used for both IJL and TSZ queues. You only use the first solve for TSZ queues, but IJL queues may have to use the second.

Then, we start with the mirroring portion. The first setup is for when you see more S or L pieces in the queue. Excluding [TIO]! queues, where the other shoe 3p is used, almost every queue will have some more pieces for the SL pair or the JZ pair. If it’s even, then both will be fine.

If you see either S or L, and it’s not a queue like SJZ where there’s more pieces for the JZ pair, this setup will have these four solves.

The respective solves are the exact same, but mirrored. These two setups cover every queue except for \[TOI]! queues where you need this fallback setup. You’ll always be able to build one of these two setups, which, again, are mirrored.

Z before L Z last   J last, L before Z   S last, L before Z
## IOSZ 
IOSZ is a rather weird yet… endearing case? It’s a bane to most researchers trying to further efforts to increase save T percentage, yet is incredibly welcoming to newer players starting to learn queue-based setups. It leans incredibly well to queue-based setups, so much so that you never even need to use the original setup, save for when the queue-based setup is an extension of it!  
I’d check out the [h-docs page](https://hsterts.github.io/h-docs/perfect-clears/2nd/ISZO/) for this PC, as it just looks nicer.
# Even JL, with T
## TIJL 
TIJL is the best with-T PC, being near-exactly on par with IJLO. It also has a strikingly similar structure, which surprised me. 
![](https://lh7-rt.googleusercontent.com/docsz/AD_4nXf4ALEzABRh3CtKeeCC_1bYQ67UPp8GR01S7aosmTEXcRLD71mtNMGUK0RFb8vyc4CX2P-mQ0mPO8PscyBkalJtT6Xa3HPhIz2NVQsxJdW1NsA07gZTYBmH5Bn2oUvnk8P4w9Yki0iAima5TD_QCsC4zkCP?key=rxGnIOzTXwvvF_Z1hOaPWA)![](https://lh7-rt.googleusercontent.com/docsz/AD_4nXeZluQyFDshnBpVfe3EpYWg876-A9khu0Kp5mggZnqTSVdWSDw0yqledmupEk1V1a6J7BMtMWMiI76JSKHQwlQPHnqWzEipSyKR9lYvfbt9AEgK0fTc1Q2hYoogAQO0qfEzb0JY8PT_qAD_5tvKncCi2wHw?key=rxGnIOzTXwvvF_Z1hOaPWA)![](https://lh7-rt.googleusercontent.com/docsz/AD_4nXcuPh3q7TI5etqJyEsybAFbJxt5qYimUdr9vtg8_0oBSWf63Y__A71CS38pK1i53WjMa9aPRTAz1TNDuwPOMQgGhEog5Gi7dODBrmfRTx3QCJRYiyesDZBuB0Y9keZE9w5MAtxT91ekqM0LjStVsaxOtC-k?key=rxGnIOzTXwvvF_Z1hOaPWA)
See L, L before O or S. Save O. Fails on \[OS]!,L queues.  
![](https://lh7-rt.googleusercontent.com/docsz/AD_4nXfCy-cdtj54UnaeYczD2bh5eRgqN7lfNbMFI_d5adzHsMdOKrmion5YnkODu0vMv9Xq9sLpQetJLrRig6Mwb7yeE6_YmIMqex_0sgaX34PxckrK5fpcJ3iR6TRQAi9Y_DJO7mxbhcPToZ7PrUZr0KMp5toX?key=rxGnIOzTXwvvF_Z1hOaPWA)![](https://lh7-rt.googleusercontent.com/docsz/AD_4nXdh6rOzHMC13XQh43iJd50vFFO6T0BdRA7TT8f0jszD-WcEgnW9hrHfP_2LuFRqFeJawpnzobHZ9uQWPgJOk-HbAxz1oLPX1gY34qG2KhRZr65VxNT5on3l9ec510LiZQheEFC_9J09vNwSh3-Lh-gN-j4i?key=rxGnIOzTXwvvF_Z1hOaPWA)![](https://lh7-rt.googleusercontent.com/docsz/AD_4nXfX5CxpELNA-jOwC0o42gH1Bh69KCMtPCQgmKxq2oX80_dcGCy6JFbEOgnBrT5mP20vw0wi2bwdlUbLbUalZ9UeqWa4z3FSw-tLO4fPBbIDyXy8Yl7VyrZDdmoaZJdaJvgWYBfSjlioMbjyBy0rXVw2KOk?key=rxGnIOzTXwvvF_Z1hOaPWA)  
See J, J before O or Z. Save O. Fails on \[OZ]!,J queues.  
![](https://lh7-rt.googleusercontent.com/docsz/AD_4nXduDk1Y4VJLL_yK_csJXOgHDpJ5OTcfdX4APay7dz15N4-FM3IjlbAicMRnWrvncwsm1uJ-Kyf7EmVRs4YLVSCYRHWGZGUUxXMdyl7Pa5waXiiunuFSs7F__BHe0ti3PL_iisjdK1Etqlta8PuSyTu64mWm?key=rxGnIOzTXwvvF_Z1hOaPWA)![](https://lh7-rt.googleusercontent.com/docsz/AD_4nXfSzeClvFWkCPDk2zt2aSbeWt5V5HeUp5XUinZmp_NXk1rmwFDT3hxotVNhg6cy5Ll0AZvEwuwE2rh5uXfDEBNVcSpzPrmhNhzIkdfMlNT5kpMVMblaECKVVJFm9qBhDA-s9EnYSUYoXqUdtiVO9UoNfKfB?key=rxGnIOzTXwvvF_Z1hOaPWA)![](https://lh7-rt.googleusercontent.com/docsz/AD_4nXdnKsy_Wo_QJKPtEWvTg4d2ABsQOF8ti_Ixd5wq_TTZWkvrLa02bqmivhItaQedzXusp8QcFVdblXBNtzXRnADU9XK0J1xfWzFMQkFYXPaOEsnwX_Kt-z3HJGtZ47K_rNZU73fhg6BVdmk8vaI1EUZLOY8?key=rxGnIOzTXwvvF_Z1hOaPWA)  
![](https://lh7-rt.googleusercontent.com/docsz/AD_4nXeGWYH1PMfqmygSZh5dJQ_HNKLbXjwLvLfOKfSLRAIBndE6dumTE2wh7IJRz8AowS5GVW8njVbIjU5Yn0VZbayuzg-EqHhfTbqiSH8STHVBHRcP9bKwuk9_nub_WXCaLRi4MR5QRE03LknKKWcUjbrwXMZz?key=rxGnIOzTXwvvF_Z1hOaPWA)![](https://lh7-rt.googleusercontent.com/docsz/AD_4nXd_5ceUxblgbE-twDPA2r3DbtYPTqgXXkdI61iklqfH_mMPYSJPIKtCXvmRXIAHuvlm20kfQpaQc3wFYupuVP96wE1cCltV8Eg_WBglaHtCspUk3q8VJLcr9UZM4YNg3FIbq4gsmJ-fALxCoYBVGXKeFH8l?key=rxGnIOzTXwvvF_Z1hOaPWA)![](https://lh7-rt.googleusercontent.com/docsz/AD_4nXfKeMFc2U-rmyZIHlAy7-NtHCG_c4amwnMpL_i9WX1d3uujT0O8gMSrtVCxzgwi9z71hin4rjpJ6tS8StRveNkU4zJYL-MlGq4Y4lheRzqE6Xx2g3yxJF3p8ldxJ3zk1chaz9ycGv2VBJj1wK--GaMBjYsD?key=rxGnIOzTXwvvF_Z1hOaPWA)  
See OZ and OS queue-based setups. They’re there to both combat fail queues in the fallback setup and the original one-piece queue-based setups.  
If you can’t build either of them, then this setup will have two solves.  
![](https://lh7-rt.googleusercontent.com/docsz/AD_4nXfHSs7Z7rUL3Be376EedeqQheB5UTnbgW_u3WaYEA7s3t9YWa9w15NJSIieLHkHK-Mhfm_7LIyaRaSOYr3blZ7KVNCMZwxRfFd7EY3zWU-ksBYFF6v4WbOblDkUhNjXLqj26yQN8UdUyV4wWwlOESBEjjE?key=rxGnIOzTXwvvF_Z1hOaPWA)  
![](https://lh7-rt.googleusercontent.com/docsz/AD_4nXfxfz2n8enkTDr8pgnkZT1eCBewcL3LW6msj1BaNZiS_ihDLf5YxPmnbidAVJN9ml64aOle-AvRcZrBCffDk-jdwrSzn1EtKWjNRjI0COvn0G15mnlCokWi8AArppgbTU9TVMg5DK0d4g2r3QiPn0mGC7md?key=rxGnIOzTXwvvF_Z1hOaPWA)![](https://lh7-rt.googleusercontent.com/docsz/AD_4nXd4jRiRTfX1C9BA1KcvGdDSqd7zLMI2rLzNtu7IMUAIZZGjfk6xOs8VRAwYh67eThFlbVAzvxakDOLHBc_FskHe4840MkFZycgzqfkbb9lnx1d4xcWL2X2GZE_qBPLPEtbVwjFTBEttJtG_sk9c-vx-StxS?key=rxGnIOzTXwvvF_Z1hOaPWA)  
But, this method is a little bit more rough around the edges than IJLO’s. There’s some weird skim orders that you need to watch out for, especially for queues like \[ISZ]!. Look out for stuff like this:

![](https://lh7-rt.googleusercontent.com/docsz/AD_4nXeZ6ogsx1dl5f_DBfCoN9aQVV9RUvNxIswVxWT5BvY1Vc-681_-ONjZ_fNHHtnGKU0oIYvAMoIHnSySHLZ8z837Kz9QclhoOSpy3Qeq2xVXJd5encCsIErVJn-Rv0sLZQU17bwh6asq4GrvfBd3OyRjeswP?key=rxGnIOzTXwvvF_Z1hOaPWA)![](https://lh7-rt.googleusercontent.com/docsz/AD_4nXcCEsbtqIg2zDVRawZcUk8lDSxPNpqU5qLwYu3BDvqqP5SWnTlRWSW7JJPTNkKxmzAq_hzSZ_ur-j8ZSZCHKYhKUSVBsaQjKXqIEpB9N9PGTxPVfpp6M2Q70v4-1miYxsRuYeHuTF3D9TGFq9P2Xq9v00rK?key=rxGnIOzTXwvvF_Z1hOaPWA)![](https://lh7-rt.googleusercontent.com/docsz/AD_4nXc7NGfyIEkvg2qhk3aBdxx6bvi4ExP0r-SFfU54CvT4KcrO5GwxlHCaAY54N3rm6MY2Xskt0Xha50DI8ltqjrSzI3COjagGbXJH-tWyJgOxWd8U-M-DL8KV8CUwIlFMcI99_HiXdC6B4jzkobNSLRCI5eUM?key=rxGnIOzTXwvvF_Z1hOaPWA)
## TIJL-extra
TIJL is one of the only odd-T PCs that are 100% T, which means that a method that prioritizes O saving might be too low-end for some players. These are some known save-T queue-based setups.
![](https://lh7-rt.googleusercontent.com/docsz/AD_4nXfid67BemD1rAzES18bYPt5Cf9kovbG3Kah7kmN4jPla7P8CHzRvqPVcHE2U9fCVhhjVDrU0QHyFFo7bAJSQ43Ah24kHiLwCcfVzWXNDcO0FR8qpQDddYVq8Pj9fJ7TY5uNYrSY5U3eScKpVECxY-ueyfM?key=rxGnIOzTXwvvF_Z1hOaPWA)![](https://lh7-rt.googleusercontent.com/docsz/AD_4nXdcnXw3vYsCVIAPSHVqr8Ac5hyQ1ae2y_fvCtvRpkHl38uRuu_2zkZLTz1P7NvaHEXERTmebD7HFAVhRdKGAdZF9v-ymoOqzmldtH4EWJg0oNjEhvetFJR3ypzMlqMgQ7YcvHoExmOKPY0p-N2fCGdoP-wU?key=rxGnIOzTXwvvF_Z1hOaPWA)![](https://lh7-rt.googleusercontent.com/docsz/AD_4nXcTwgSI1kfootQFNUTo4l_eTWcFPLNyyelw-18I0miUGT4SRMhV4dAIqVteTTErtPzTZ8P9nmIvksRuZZUGGF4ND1KS2nPt_8DbVazJFY0iR-EOdUky233LgkEpviOqnLtCV3e_qfaBxsbhSE-xy3ftaLU?key=rxGnIOzTXwvvF_Z1hOaPWA)
JS queue-based setup. I remember it by making the JS shape in my head on the left-hand side, and seeing how TIJL must fit to finish the shape.
![](https://lh7-rt.googleusercontent.com/docsz/AD_4nXfF4kJ2ZKCF-90_06QoBtJA5xlY_PnPlkt8j4cyr-rRPaqdIYNJosN2EAKofyTqv6LHrjYW3vV8wo5UXVDDFtLrxsStlz79YZxJiRz-vnLD504TXyqiVQaH1VmFvgiwfeXGBn8haxoMHUpVDG5OujxxFds?key=rxGnIOzTXwvvF_Z1hOaPWA)![](https://lh7-rt.googleusercontent.com/docsz/AD_4nXd9TpYajBOWclA08Li7prTl0_cIMZt-C4pHERV7cCIgq3jGx80GVRf5EudHUnIxET6EKsJFwIY4zvAetuiIw7gzMisBMenS9n5S7JytMHeYxzgOGQ54zy95IygAVoiPjiyhzeCCZRhRr7fzCD-PN33V_yR2?key=rxGnIOzTXwvvF_Z1hOaPWA)![](https://lh7-rt.googleusercontent.com/docsz/AD_4nXdKOmrlm40_9znFCBfk1guouq2H2fDGikaSz08CXDEkper0ELtSyc8K1lNtTCRaGVqIThRJk5SnYp9k8iYNcAL2x9ejPKer1XSZD0avMbVK_1M2FwmWo3GlYIozekruhoZzzDw8wP3THI-t-RK9lLqUDwno?key=rxGnIOzTXwvvF_Z1hOaPWA)
IS queue-based setup. It’s ramp, which is seen in TJLS save T sometimes. Hold the T and 180 the L in, or just use the other way to build the LJ shape.
![](https://lh7-rt.googleusercontent.com/docsz/AD_4nXcYBdLVAw9HOr5ACvqjm1eTpudlbO39aJIHPqGQhoil8wRikTf9MxoJw2bQuq-b1z2bp8pNi8_J0Icph_58qa3_aTdmWM6E0dswU8z6N9N4YYfSr0Mk8Bgr2kmk-9iPO74lPbadYQwtt3Ikn-epOgGCs6w?key=rxGnIOzTXwvvF_Z1hOaPWA)![](https://lh7-rt.googleusercontent.com/docsz/AD_4nXdO5M3iPXU_Qv9IFiaU12SglUfUdasa6iCsD__JecuZbyLbZA2McLVqBeJd0_AdH-qbVT2lGB8hQXPZhF9K3JiXuiVh0Ti5eLS3GjqwLEjiEmfZNkvSeMkBt3d3MqtpbShOBOMkjuBZ3YsnxymB85ygACiG?key=rxGnIOzTXwvvF_Z1hOaPWA)![](https://lh7-rt.googleusercontent.com/docsz/AD_4nXc6ks97MwHsvXYwDHMIpce3p1QNo-PPsBtrPNje1YHHIN_KSz2biTgq8xb659HRavY0vG4Ypn7VnKkYktrD1DYNChokke6_jgLbLqIT8d8aVwnBj8kSKe51ouJaKU_6bBjDzmhx-YCLFxctzZ4pZAUVGnBn?key=rxGnIOzTXwvvF_Z1hOaPWA)
OS queue-based setup. Technically a congruent to Heart + PCO, and very similar to JLOS-OS as well.
![](https://lh7-rt.googleusercontent.com/docsz/AD_4nXd8EONlrqwt7to-EL5_gxLF-tT4kr8OItbU8IVZ8cE2BSTz1NgGAibTEB6yRMCSPgk69mqoUGDZuZ1aP_5cOJdQ4KmsgUJlZ5YTsjNgWsh8PeTudT3mm2aOoEsaaT_qzNGjGogUvIy8E0B62DxnhvjkHAyl?key=rxGnIOzTXwvvF_Z1hOaPWA)![](https://lh7-rt.googleusercontent.com/docsz/AD_4nXf-b3d9LugBMn3-j84O58ZCN8iRbhB1ultNTh6R3EQ9IE0DFg4_QpumdCVuJPznnFeQGhksrQWLDmV694hZAGB8IfWVF29Lm5xE6XMEBLk-tBbSpk3I4AfW0N8CpcGII01Tk-wcX8CpNmjnxcRTs50UyNt7?key=rxGnIOzTXwvvF_Z1hOaPWA)![](https://lh7-rt.googleusercontent.com/docsz/AD_4nXcw_zpmw7Glthfp5IJ5Or8d56qVL7go9kwbYhP-z8-yPRsFd2uLyn4E5AMsooqf1kkc0JpQ9zD8gRabLRdkMAlkxZ08gwxiHEOdIx1-S917vmN6bIsXE7MqENuZZ5k1Gz2p5Q58Fzi043TIbLMz3fUY0TA?key=rxGnIOzTXwvvF_Z1hOaPWA)  
SZ, S before Z queue-based setup. Another setup where the two queue-based placements are memorable enough to help you determine the shape itself. 
![](https://lh7-rt.googleusercontent.com/docsz/AD_4nXeKyV8mz3twrHo53RPibqEWnBTxh93SD04ieu47Xxl4VfKkUa70A9x8Gvy0xXdNtZaPOWOjh6BjNVCJyfStFZC2Hk5AMkqqR8bH6YkNdJkYL_LU5BxbM5UwOt2v_O7aoJMKCNx2tP3CDMsPSTSf-UyvzfE?key=rxGnIOzTXwvvF_Z1hOaPWA)![](https://lh7-rt.googleusercontent.com/docsz/AD_4nXfokKQCBK1N32Wm-wXwJ1bk-vAbMxLpmrRHCi69CdAd6bScFfwwqzcKC9U1BLHP02L-DSvU_AMHfF08GNlzcd5iQGfVRNSAhkFPt_izJMUYl96A31mTB-50gvwKzajmW192wkCoNds87tEA1fIVOWpryWA?key=rxGnIOzTXwvvF_Z1hOaPWA)![](https://lh7-rt.googleusercontent.com/docsz/AD_4nXcU9iT6cRLMTJ1WM49MzlKHQPf2hrWJTULdz3oZhIhWM5JexSYZD2xuifeD4-Jj8TiaEv-jHC5ZpNbDXqELGtDkF4LId7vfPHXVadoocIUgS07rJKZ_LYzyti0BdB-eyJDiiMgJycaLvmmtj2O4L0Z90QXn?key=rxGnIOzTXwvvF_Z1hOaPWA)  
OJ queue-based setup. Notably, the same precursor shape is used on TISZ for save T as well.}  
A link to a method to get every possible bit of save T out of TIJL is showcased [here](https://docs.google.com/document/d/13RJEuctlLiyWRE1c1ROZTpTZPmPDFFZkqjRBNoUcTbw/edit).
## TIJL-T/I
This method hinges on the use of the setups mentioned in the TIJL-extra portion above. This intends to finish off the queues not covered with easy save T with save I solves. You reach 80% save T on TIJL with the above setups and fail on queues comprised of \[TIJL]p3, \[TLS]!, and \[TIO]! queues. There does exist a save T queue-based setup for when S is before L, but that doesn’t cover queues like TLS.
## TJLO*
TJLO is surprisingly not that good for the fact that it has two JL and a T piece. Any of its good setups are never 100% buildable. It does have its mirroring ability making up for it, though.
![](https://lh7-rt.googleusercontent.com/docsz/AD_4nXf_D33cjeCCW41fkm43eNEugHFFHSb5nZFnWqKhfVyHIJ5zqr8kl4pSEO-melCopmZCrlW_Kv7wO-fyxQUX6mD9tPIkyVQ6FsEHpSqoOuzkMipEcwYBUD37OrFMCIGUBMG4zSYAPBqfg8wi_zCf3ir9yLQ?key=rxGnIOzTXwvvF_Z1hOaPWA)
![](https://lh7-rt.googleusercontent.com/docsz/AD_4nXfHV5VZF3H0JI4J_V5tMbAqY5G1THwqU6TTHrQostZnu96nKOjP9zzd0GNX9aJyzulmiZGnXVqufp-EURc1pMmqaPh7oBVBsqVbPo2M9t_BVfzR6VfOWj2R8tZgHueJktaAJPo4ebnc8T2dr1rSWS8QKsAs?key=rxGnIOzTXwvvF_Z1hOaPWA)![](https://lh7-rt.googleusercontent.com/docsz/AD_4nXfoeWV8KzeYrJoVQdf6kCMeTkMOW77-3Q_KIaw8VncxIPkiMdjIZbSjmm4tgdkDrZgn5WYImWKQaYjXXYMcjT43Cx8uVBnVUk1yP6yZBtU8iZeXXD72_bd-UZAqgNHpigSiV1ZyznqNMlHpe60dPVIRPuM?key=rxGnIOzTXwvvF_Z1hOaPWA)![](https://lh7-rt.googleusercontent.com/docsz/AD_4nXcrfgTHw1-z1AK87bNNeVznucTOQTdPer5A5d1poihLiuV6cDU0SZqUKamdRsf2aJIvBav_GRazAQCWU0KtYehGpjQN3VVkwH4WDbXsqBgIn-B5UAKIZ_UFkVb1BsrTEOMIMqA8GnV9C7SyZj7J35thlOdV?key=rxGnIOzTXwvvF_Z1hOaPWA)![](https://lh7-rt.googleusercontent.com/docsz/AD_4nXcg0kfS-MZfbIF17YHApX2vvKf-5owNLAuKgHpYEfyQmqKbztNBlUMxw9rrjS5CYc8ufmlnuo2ieNNRusroIGUojjTQDEYMmowbeJFzOS9msWyoLUnhA9FZyZKL97qwQmh7ZcFinbgtGGhTcLIoUPtQ3xm_?key=rxGnIOzTXwvvF_Z1hOaPWA)
This is the see Z before S queue-based setup. The last solve is only needed on \[TIZ]! queues when you reveal O, and can be substituted with a save T queue-based setup if you are inclined to do so. The first solve has an incredible 91% cover.
![](https://lh7-rt.googleusercontent.com/docsz/AD_4nXecug9AMKNJm0ZZNawzwRi50UcpvWRb0qvT3hAXA_mxyiBmSE8cAq772UPx5FE_8ect39Uzw-qHCCu6JPMz_lFH_PxL-KiaMrXGBmd81WA1P3K-ZY8nbusY80RxIqUcXosD8M3O7YQ_NBrWshZTvK0RIrlt?key=rxGnIOzTXwvvF_Z1hOaPWA)
![](https://lh7-rt.googleusercontent.com/docsz/AD_4nXerBYT5ZPzkEm2_eeg2uUU-N0se9z_E7CbhKxrGCdewVnf37rZsSHZmbrQFXD-57j0kX2Yg20LL4SlVLd8UhUt5fYhqlTpcICfYmIR-DKSf1_7Di3J8qammCak7IknMCIAfGIgXUm7Iqh3PUcB25-oJx436?key=rxGnIOzTXwvvF_Z1hOaPWA)![](https://lh7-rt.googleusercontent.com/docsz/AD_4nXdPCW9EhoipA067l7Vsm2M3ojqj2zFPyopM2dMJPkFOGjIhfHejgg2FIgsMzTjMiPTn_EMT4wKuN6FfNMjIIDVVyKWCAr4mwumKchkX71b6oJ0ytHkoMqKqeEuvDw69BPM1zvCsreXWMsNDCRE6jHf_1itA?key=rxGnIOzTXwvvF_Z1hOaPWA)![](https://lh7-rt.googleusercontent.com/docsz/AD_4nXeh9hXiDVUpqum63fPu8vVS-HccSnvypXGsvIb8IcnFo4l7quH4gTsSSiX3sSegGhQjNdg5mqDfUXc0MnKcx_1QvKdDMoNN1we3E_do1Y5n6IF2jlHokRGrZw2JA7a3FOMxK1Z535j0Pgd_5K3Sj9zIxOtw?key=rxGnIOzTXwvvF_Z1hOaPWA)![](https://lh7-rt.googleusercontent.com/docsz/AD_4nXf16wyTUFGQ_v8prPiC_NvWa09N9u_hY1BD7sjECsRL6IuqGrMi3t_Aa3kR5Zjl0R0SGoi5DKLUVcFY23OZ9izRPZ67WREAufHdDDuwHK9q4f-KIL--o1rFrY-0s6tNebViBsc5kGEtEPUXWjfoJeBk-BVf?key=rxGnIOzTXwvvF_Z1hOaPWA)
If you read this document before TJLO’s renovation (yes, there was a method before this), then you might notice that this setup is simply a partial of 3 of the different see S or Z queue-based setups.

Then, there are the IJ and IL queue-based setups, to mitigate fail queues for the fallback setup. If you can’t build it (on queues like OLI or SLI) then the second set of queue-based setups will be applicable, or the SI/ZI queue-based setups.  
![](https://lh7-rt.googleusercontent.com/docsz/AD_4nXci2SkqngHDNh9fD7ozcDyyiEFxIRj70-Oj8OiB9ZxawspFY9PZqVsfg6upFw-JlEufclYgqjNGkfhG8dLM_NANzoyYx4ETeAbw7drwpTxHJh4OMyWeT31OWxmr_2HlGLAwhkVzU1KiPFQcVxT3EtnVIXKx?key=rxGnIOzTXwvvF_Z1hOaPWA)![](https://lh7-rt.googleusercontent.com/docsz/AD_4nXc57n3PQPagL0gL7zrsEjixxsQ5sBvX8fecdzU6bmM9hs0UbEGjz7A5hTpXXLqUomz4ZcQAWKwYBQ4BOiCxnpv0WdsxCdivc1BhuJW6Lkt4vgWnwgqQWei9rL4Qe1_eNtKx6qwr7URw-4TSoYaFb3O7fmk?key=rxGnIOzTXwvvF_Z1hOaPWA)![](https://lh7-rt.googleusercontent.com/docsz/AD_4nXdW-f8ACiGtARDTjYI2WNEhItV5pgxONqhXJeZB1hnQC-96nFnzB7YjJtJPX6x-ivi4HYRwlvRg-y_prDUDVwyuaX-Dn3cDrIDtGaepL66y22iDQN9hrYWuKTY7yeLrX9t2uYVD0u_zxArjJa7RTCQFcWL7?key=rxGnIOzTXwvvF_Z1hOaPWA)

These save O.

These save T.  
Then, there’s the weird queue-based setups- JLO and JLT.  
![](https://lh7-rt.googleusercontent.com/docsz/AD_4nXcZ9AqQJLFPdMRQmpPLv_Yq_yZsCdLF2TUq3In8oY-vhi9CXtyMyP8e-0sHI3NRYeKNsnUgqPwbg8V7aZ9eDUVGu9uoD_hc-x9VwHbgCgufQivsfbOa6XP0W1B7gfCor1BD1BgpU8soy5tZPXZWhm-n3Rw?key=rxGnIOzTXwvvF_Z1hOaPWA)![](https://lh7-rt.googleusercontent.com/docsz/AD_4nXfWnj2R91rQMcAq-b3nM5YksjxurLD_dfZlYyDbWYpFFUDtARQj_lnvKd8fK4lAKmMjTw5aHj84a3bcmaiOytMTQ2ojjGmwM7AXEN5R9DcWRcYqignJGESZr5ch8hr5qIAaapxC8xqe8pZQzo_rrstFa9nl?key=rxGnIOzTXwvvF_Z1hOaPWA)![](https://lh7-rt.googleusercontent.com/docsz/AD_4nXfQU3qYP6jFuWaf5VsdaWGUdIqPYNU3Liym_y0POPtarNL_biA3dtfEzf9yyUou7Aps63iSqR6NkQC11pJq5WaWnpMVT5SC4ShsfAozDfGqrQbyxyEr2NxFaANUSaW4qXs1dfFH4ySuiEc7UfyUnaIKj3Y?key=rxGnIOzTXwvvF_Z1hOaPWA)  
No 100% build one-solve queue-based setup exists for JLO, so this is the next best thing. Choose the solution based on SZ order.  
![](https://lh7-rt.googleusercontent.com/docsz/AD_4nXdyb9g2aA642ZCxDEokmgYSECHk7gP1fZO7JyKALgFRJ_He-ff2VBxdmJ3RVQ8Xxg2ZQvkuCNeFH3BR2IKqfSmQKCMmIzd7qbpD8zeNvoziEXlzL2FNjnMu23Y1n2M1RQQ7MBLcInPrtML_vfeTGIT5_x6b?key=rxGnIOzTXwvvF_Z1hOaPWA)![](https://lh7-rt.googleusercontent.com/docsz/AD_4nXfBbRf7hkYxOyZhnMnWFPnE9S2JSqeOycEpHKDw7NVxcWanTb4bITyA_yA4rIdhSGeQNWsHPnyR72FYBo0YAKeiJarSeMEWfNAPfF-zR1kqFgG2S3boXxAplrPvCdxmEIRdMEW6PKavoQi4wxKlIHf3GgPT?key=rxGnIOzTXwvvF_Z1hOaPWA)![](https://lh7-rt.googleusercontent.com/docsz/AD_4nXcyjfr8diFdbTj5QqQu-A6vffxcJo_lAlfTUkGfoQ98D89B2F8Xa36-SWytCjlGfJpofyBkyZnExci4EhEcRKQPtNsZmCt80tajwtz0JmzR7SCylWcjyInTPNu1m4hk2ugLswLBD6xaGKYxgZUFw-RSLkg?key=rxGnIOzTXwvvF_Z1hOaPWA)  
This saves O. From now on, for queues like \[TJO]!,\[TLO]!, and \[TIO]!, we have to compromise for save I.  
![](https://lh7-rt.googleusercontent.com/docsz/AD_4nXffGpj6M2F5Gfp08FTNKUzqkNK9UFQQ9o-HhAmDBEu4Itt7n97Q4_rQpmVklY813WnOGQt2SvaXADaCqrmWQ6J02lwezRoN4q6MzcdjiG2vgqIYhT5qNnH5Ty5QIDarwYNqCFs6n35QvCaB936x2geQudYv?key=rxGnIOzTXwvvF_Z1hOaPWA)![](https://lh7-rt.googleusercontent.com/docsz/AD_4nXcrob7lfq3ZmmjNx6J7Q0E7VBHxE7LqdZqxFWbu1YBEeSHGXJ2XEfcGD30TtivnQEsh_Qp5S_T3GCjx7U8dnw-03YBXdN36LDg6vCg8mBcuRhAIAud0bgG2FXaBV-AzAkx-oSO9T0EjQUjJh_fmi35qiMk?key=rxGnIOzTXwvvF_Z1hOaPWA)  
![](https://lh7-rt.googleusercontent.com/docsz/AD_4nXdGUHTrbFscMU9EPdNljvDShwJ00nzrhJ1R1QVq3bfREOBlmrSp9YVNF28RA8gr4Ri6A5jrWah7_IRpAdK7C2lBLVKEkrosScTnPlrq6tVemj_ehLW9RvGKVzGaMWOmLTJJ5Z81nn_sGUYQjJVTG2dlBH9t?key=rxGnIOzTXwvvF_Z1hOaPWA)![](https://lh7-rt.googleusercontent.com/docsz/AD_4nXenVBQGrxb5s7_BfUgrHsJeOv6u8VDviTHXQodip3sMsQWoVMtj56Bpkd_8753OmGRj7g1Zem1jIDOkXL81OddKwczDgX0riPxaog9IngB3yiP3jtwenRXbN--sdgfCQhK9vdrFjzhxwudY3Tsa4ZWBkzgz?key=rxGnIOzTXwvvF_Z1hOaPWA)![](https://lh7-rt.googleusercontent.com/docsz/AD_4nXe24XKupHzO5wpTt8PTrkSss6Y6ZXT5_a3USEyUpcdbRKLtcsfFGEqear58hVR1KLfzQFjxDPY7VMDpAJ2Vtt7LICFx2jmdAAEyPFFKJv7O9xVuF20rjXF8y-WrYsysH7J9irWvy_uGgq90Nq8UXW699JpN?key=rxGnIOzTXwvvF_Z1hOaPWA)  
You can luck into save O sometimes with this setup, but for queues like OJT, you have to place the O and take the third solve.  
## TJLO-extra
These are some extra setups to reach 100% O/T on TJLO.  
To replace the setups used on \[TLO]! and \[TLJ]!, you can use this:

Then these four solves are for S last (first 2) and Z last (last 2) where the queue reading is based on JL order (L,J for save T; J,L for save O)
## TISZ 

TISZ can also be approached similarly to IOSZ. It’s possibly also one of the easiest 2nd PCs to 100% TO, with a total of six setups without mirror to fully cover. It also has an [h-docs page](https://hsterts.github.io/h-docs/perfect-clears/2nd/TISZ/), which I partially wrote! The LO queue-based setup is entirely unnecessary, you can omit that from your learning. Here’s a slightly edited version that I made.  
![](https://lh7-rt.googleusercontent.com/docsz/AD_4nXflJqJIRAXPNtTOw4-TlXWt7Qc7_Y6lNtg0RfS5uzRtk_byXQB4JaQDtkDafD2JF1INanhXMOUM77CVZjk-omDPUhu2ha1Y5m-a-rQ_RINktOsYEo79lT1Fp1FtnH9vN7ajRe-NDtH7CantR53laI1IMsc?key=rxGnIOzTXwvvF_Z1hOaPWA)![](https://lh7-rt.googleusercontent.com/docsz/AD_4nXeTXtaf4h8oF91yvgsavrfEX7BGBLi4XI3cQS-eWEqoZZQj-YrhMrwlRi7GEAgt8zXho11Y7hjCs6aOPDxWt3na94OgRkieTviMXPPe69SKYLYyD_-MGZAFlwvV8r1lHJBmOQwSkCRHRVptmBEhc_S0MJcp?key=rxGnIOzTXwvvF_Z1hOaPWA)![](https://lh7-rt.googleusercontent.com/docsz/AD_4nXc4XfIs_EmZHGtrx9j1mTyUtiVyxhi1K-7KI6XezZNS1pZDRtfZpk7T9YANV8hGv9hBI72pT06cUqCMmQ0TkqHk3vUw93C6N0cRNUIbXeuKUHmI7anI9wRYf6Moyds_uLt46f8wKRIVrQGXBQ98em-YdYrr?key=rxGnIOzTXwvvF_Z1hOaPWA)  
![](https://lh7-rt.googleusercontent.com/docsz/AD_4nXesK2omECQllarL4CyHuJc6ITOldKHREZTjoE-TMoeMtfWHT15mgJyK005EkSIvfiH2OphYKv9LsiXIY9TVetXUiS4B4F8DIOwUdARVY-_pJrpuLZVDd3yj679egDCHJ3NyJTAuSSYFijRPDIgWBO6BXI23?key=rxGnIOzTXwvvF_Z1hOaPWA)![](https://lh7-rt.googleusercontent.com/docsz/AD_4nXf484EdHmlgFxtDbuVw9Q0ZvxVWhjkI7VmmsbJmaitAZo7vEeuW80HH0h_FK0AAW_mdlgRxfbh1nBTGw3K5kkQXD7oiipCmAggcU0Q846A49dIhWo2ViuqBDk2hzVB-tCPQIXoIATN7zLhcirguwW0GjjGc?key=rxGnIOzTXwvvF_Z1hOaPWA)![](https://lh7-rt.googleusercontent.com/docsz/AD_4nXfcDt6lMS_FGA-2UK-JxtofgSinY0Q1DXjkrbsvCsOHF_LOTS9TpNdeYaos_i-oE729nVsytj6CyasXu7BlhmC0jEeIQCUj_rDoP22A7RrM6u78Q84KL9yju3WEkaW59HXBaPGKsIF3r8w6RDv1CBSFJE7F?key=rxGnIOzTXwvvF_Z1hOaPWA)

L and J queue-based setups, respectively. Fails on \[SO]!,L and \[ZO]!,J queues respectively.  
![](https://lh7-rt.googleusercontent.com/docsz/AD_4nXck0pB21euuxe2OnGded9vVo6-hOG2c0QaLCQxbeAXycoTLMs0iieO_6LzPn12KIc8TZXwCes8-YF222W3a5mLwhK5jkitQkWfhRL2EzZ02ewBejFmB6mhcCXP6jy6lJc3HUBVHcw1RZLqUc_Dc17IHzdTp?key=rxGnIOzTXwvvF_Z1hOaPWA)![](https://lh7-rt.googleusercontent.com/docsz/AD_4nXdmwBInHYCFwEKUUE2qZU4MCrcgjigVoW5tG0Ej7ejKySLFOQJRvCUZ3WvGGe3U_Cq5eWf5BEq5EEjKqsoPmEw9LYItUoIRqst7NsJGdgGqBGnU6314m0BDjVhimuZA6rZIEGRAEaL76tHTSZ55d7UJwipZ?key=rxGnIOzTXwvvF_Z1hOaPWA)![](https://lh7-rt.googleusercontent.com/docsz/AD_4nXdZkhd2fnPhW6Xht0ETqzU5lY3WpZuq1jax0M3oAj53bVuqcg2Ba0hcbCnD7iapCkPirgwabENb0b2__7VPy7FU11itclm66cn4rMEzvib3D64iRW0UGrHvq1gIkNzZgqxIAd5N3T_4sFA2g0y9U9WDJpM?key=rxGnIOzTXwvvF_Z1hOaPWA)

The only thing I’d change is the ISZ queue-based setup. It’s easier to remember, where you place the two groups of ISZ while holding T until the end. It’s still the same result.
## TOSZ*
I hate TOSZ. I can’t even give you a 100% O/T method, because I’ve barely even made it 99.64% save O/T. It is the only 2nd PC to need OQB to achieve 100% O/T.  
![](https://lh7-rt.googleusercontent.com/docsz/AD_4nXfCDN_0_0Snkiz1ro6jJTrYiC9vB-CrIlpcAwDkriFtxsUQmv7HM6HDqo_MtkSd1zfq7L-I5xFQrvVuQ8ub1x2eDJi2Hz8DO_OrKfosn9xHYDgqzDcg3hP1AYFBSJEFNVrhPDgpKFU6Tq1XZHgWbIflxwsp?key=rxGnIOzTXwvvF_Z1hOaPWA)![](https://lh7-rt.googleusercontent.com/docsz/AD_4nXeqxZ19AR96cGajp8huXwmLXVmkWA4IC-ylMktJfqjo2b6ZUwyuqHG7MtJGosAeoVyhVuTeeRV8stnOPHYPv7xDYcilk8KOuCN60_n_Pa9hjsKWiCONTiEns5gOudu_6ujf4Fc4zHfa6_EVNZdl2Z3pf2A0?key=rxGnIOzTXwvvF_Z1hOaPWA)![](https://lh7-rt.googleusercontent.com/docsz/AD_4nXcDtXZmS8IjsEpl0ergnkVsLrD95cGskoU7pMZaSwoKpGSU5gUF7PORkvk-fhcVzzYArroNUGt9fr5iN-GnjRv4kPoMfhQzCoC5-xOke0cYjDYY38Hp6hbpidf_kYzCXIoPRc8ALOfeU-XopeeomKUGB60?key=rxGnIOzTXwvvF_Z1hOaPWA)  
![](https://lh7-rt.googleusercontent.com/docsz/AD_4nXf98wd6UGKDJeJ5JXZThmCSQBgzXO6-ULlfRNvODPHaxdNcBHP4gc6M1LVhHdYV9Edh8VNBygHerrZRw_8olVyLz4EQm8dlxVFWifDykMUhC3F-fYjhGzjkxEqsK2zxxvYlLjWbcHKwzpJYcJSRfldxQqLn?key=rxGnIOzTXwvvF_Z1hOaPWA)![](https://lh7-rt.googleusercontent.com/docsz/AD_4nXdggP6Gto_vFBnZaUoV1TMEWkuaLKVv49L3Nlvz8N9c7jvdp3qQbv78_jmME_hazyD0Z8NCniRlnVJrv5XGbaN46XLziHevG-rdwIRRZVZX69pdRZ6fLYvjHcJc8wwXzBxA_EQs9fxdX15E1xF8wGpKslV7?key=rxGnIOzTXwvvF_Z1hOaPWA)![](https://lh7-rt.googleusercontent.com/docsz/AD_4nXe4dkRdBxU-vb3IZTUJBrL9CJw0qUZIeA0-uxyWGY5v1nRJflSP1zd28c3VqfWDE7Zu9h0tJNBAMWA3gnNkSRiTwrfP-oi9TySf3CwxJ2UzpQeT0nsX6id42H-sq0Vb5HdIFw5JXPDKenaXgYMM9zGYnRiN?key=rxGnIOzTXwvvF_Z1hOaPWA)  
These two are the see TL/TJ save O setups. Then, I’m going to advise you to pray.  
![](https://lh7-rt.googleusercontent.com/docsz/AD_4nXdoIqyJW06Y_ja_gXj1C75PzTmSRKdHfKAG-y7_okbl9j8LgFDg6CQ8pEJNhOPA1YAQguahQgbrE4zzv-ipOubS58bVEIwuCfdcHdXkG8r1Wh6UhTqOCkM6-sflPAXTb-vGQrg4IeH25jR9FDSRkrbMgB4?key=rxGnIOzTXwvvF_Z1hOaPWA)  
This has about 98% T/O coverage, and if you mirror it correctly, it can get to about 99%.  
This setup would be for see L, as it has more fail queues for see J.

Then, to squeeze as much saves out of this setup, here are the two extra necessary save I solves.  
![](https://lh7-rt.googleusercontent.com/docsz/AD_4nXcTfhApenyA3etRhJxJBHaE3YPkd4e1HinI7SEsueBu_jAaJbrFGUQRHgJ0hTmPTbGBxXhQ53calZBSW8pUEl3C4UZFUxY6GMegLFjd5qAFzDUSu2GL9YRhLWJQJQxdJoBpRrCDvBue4gqI9drB_lRK2LWg?key=rxGnIOzTXwvvF_Z1hOaPWA)![](https://lh7-rt.googleusercontent.com/docsz/AD_4nXdMCDIcLW7Nh1xQvFEoIBtLBaR9EHdNd_cQvs2nGt9Dg5KlJ6UtDrOIGzSCeNFPOLvoaXpaldXAwMe7GR_oyNXOza4YSf7a5F4r7O4nVPP1NS5byWwOgrGnX2qbpqX8E4MKnZ3rNcnjrtaWVkvU?key=rxGnIOzTXwvvF_Z1hOaPWA)

## TIOS/TIOZ*
TIOS is a rather uncomfortable case for many, as it’s hard to attain high T/O rates with relative ease. Like with JLOS, we’ll be compromising to save I as well. It does have two very high cover queue-based setups, though.

![](https://lh7-rt.googleusercontent.com/docsz/AD_4nXcIjjhG8bjC4pKThaYL-D0mTGmRCWXmHv6dPlUys4q5-zdT_eIz2guQBc3PpuOYskioZCzf8ufXxRfHGZ8qgCu8kGfzWvEdNDjZJC7KJ7uQcoM9FjtYfp5exMazP-sMEFhYe3Fgn5_yThp8zcLxbrqfDEpl?key=rxGnIOzTXwvvF_Z1hOaPWA)![](https://lh7-rt.googleusercontent.com/docsz/AD_4nXcvPL_nqBFNr8qg3t-aH5qoCTgRa0mJYiQ-GqLhr2zWKlOrtLo46Y8D2k2pHOdlSU7Kvx7ZQfqRirmFyksmlK5_sNd6tbJf7si-EmBsilAMcEc7-lon44xOM-dSpVyLk1-UoXuO_EymZCsn-xX1aTfIbA8?key=rxGnIOzTXwvvF_Z1hOaPWA)![](https://lh7-rt.googleusercontent.com/docsz/AD_4nXeJn2YV0GaQc1K5M2HxwTQtIiqc8otSPa2INbaDH5prByyNUcw_KDYs84F06vQRrN_OuUGcAeKaOnj8H3AQFU5u62Nhj5bwUFHU_qGkK3oTt3QhtnMI_SWCBlA55yCw-v4gSoizSaxHNxn6UXTjfziP746w?key=rxGnIOzTXwvvF_Z1hOaPWA)  
See Z, Z before T or O. Saves O. Fails on \[OT]!,Z queues.

![](https://lh7-rt.googleusercontent.com/docsz/AD_4nXdZVmC9Bz8gzE6mtwcsTO0JQSLCRxFE4-ZLxXyxYICwKP_uUM27vBftrpTBjzLMh0aNGgOV4HrBz_FpCBzu-Omu5WACi-Q4SJvQEa1n9NA2ZJgKFXOqjIOiuAJTvGFsf-GXJQmNeHHDQZ3-m5Bk3N6Fms4f?key=rxGnIOzTXwvvF_Z1hOaPWA)![](https://lh7-rt.googleusercontent.com/docsz/AD_4nXfQCFRAJekH8HorUYYSK-0DelAvDN2vWODskuE_XcIem4zN1haYaHsYD-mqZDGiKtR_sogf9trg7_NlX7hs5dRnx-gkyaRYNW16v5qR0ILGjSfOHKnyDHZUB_C7SK5EpMYOtq58Fh5FK8G0uo3xqUnd2Tx5?key=rxGnIOzTXwvvF_Z1hOaPWA)![](https://lh7-rt.googleusercontent.com/docsz/AD_4nXc88LbtEZ04S76KCleN1wbslLGVSZM-VeFPN_nqbWQVfQtk8IOGbpnceHfNBOiHhNWxmMzdyTCIchBt03zYXDDZwm5QVPZEm_pzEESXNAwYG9in7wPrR81C-zSvXyjRGbU1l5crf6aB1AuhU9yAS1Ypu04C?key=rxGnIOzTXwvvF_Z1hOaPWA)  
See S, S before T or O. Saves O. Fails on \[OT]!,S queues.  
![](https://lh7-rt.googleusercontent.com/docsz/AD_4nXfCQRzqObzojETMXOsHHMWiMVHgLnrOmrqIGAiQTun_d7xdQ0va0nCy2uyxBgcgwxOcN5ycsEwmrb7OvaaJ-uFh9BSIf4En3F96WG-mSiOTZImzw84p3HSPxQoflNP0HczRr_K6lKD-o4rrwgCcrBajenMI?key=rxGnIOzTXwvvF_Z1hOaPWA)![](https://lh7-rt.googleusercontent.com/docsz/AD_4nXf0-_4yWfiwV4pJuXraUuowGusKhQKgyHUCD4vXwv--9YIJjla5IyJcPuMJBlvlQwte7qjIE820eibfTMof94x71R8HOXpHAFvpaa30zevcBI1xGQ7VMwPnR9ed6psPu_kQM4Igux5u4syVwu3MG0HRt_E?key=rxGnIOzTXwvvF_Z1hOaPWA)![](https://lh7-rt.googleusercontent.com/docsz/AD_4nXcOi70bEj0KwHto8_hPm8DGr4n2W3xYMSJISXHO1H80jUaNvqP1LGHrmkc0CHWu286KLRdcf5LSO8dTWbPl6PHOMLgWY0TlYHvMfm-xvUrwO2q4NoSKWPhEcJUlkfpLWAsWbKgb-TWGdOg-LddSmKQMpFQ?key=rxGnIOzTXwvvF_Z1hOaPWA)  
![](https://lh7-rt.googleusercontent.com/docsz/AD_4nXeDWmBz5Fz3THThldLuutJ4JhsIOo07bW4g6L_TTgG9Z1f3_LE_APp3IY2mYdP2zZ_klP4cmx9s7l7PbGIQxvWGiQ9P-BcKcFLmjPqTUpIjw-_gQ4X631x-vo6JCTdYzCNwoyrFavCmdEGwfnncDbIy6z8?key=rxGnIOzTXwvvF_Z1hOaPWA)![](https://lh7-rt.googleusercontent.com/docsz/AD_4nXfF-NNMme0SqmiSgSDikQQgJ93k9eetXwUNP-S7KXXizu5KDQMw9F8Mx5z_IHL3alTiTqFIVngJ9ztFMlqqnk096rdPECKYPD7OS0Plvee_LB6N-azCNPvkGI1QxP9n50h3NeObmefyxA6A58e_EvrRyS-D?key=rxGnIOzTXwvvF_Z1hOaPWA)![](https://lh7-rt.googleusercontent.com/docsz/AD_4nXdTJiJZ0sInssTIE--VfYB9N2LwfVHhw2zD98JA5sAzUcxQMn_15FggLm7cJ2oLSZestUocbnC8LI_4s3W5xk6dHSp_JOoBanoPc3tIy7NK9Bj0AN5ppcFobGtcDPMT-U3sDty-wQFGwAjp7zQxeYheneQ8?key=rxGnIOzTXwvvF_Z1hOaPWA)  
These two are the OS and TZ queue-based setups. They save T and O. There used to be a save T counterpart for \[TO]!Z queues, but it’s actually only 22/24 build cover.

To mitigate some of the fail queues (consisting of queues with IJ and IL in them) here are two more setups:  
![](https://lh7-rt.googleusercontent.com/docsz/AD_4nXczrotRkUHEpZqZkiAcVFqjgdvXAiMhOO9wuEaRv5CXKiZgOmvmhveINzKNDT0D0EoCqHpesISmbuNfIoKl3Yb9SAWsnWYDwy511o0StbRCbyIVOha4e-Y5RFZpWnToKD6ZvW417CynXkAQt1eoPaOLEbI?key=rxGnIOzTXwvvF_Z1hOaPWA)![](https://lh7-rt.googleusercontent.com/docsz/AD_4nXeW9NnELhegHnjanFe7btgjI7GRsSbLBemMwxzEoXq8BdWENfoEOL8EZLJw_vd-kvlGDs-t8ZQ1leY8JWF7Jq7u6w55NKLJaoCO6__QZKvd9C2loSsD2cAI5cIk_mqBH9zFE-M17V8AyzUHcp9A1kGZqVA?key=rxGnIOzTXwvvF_Z1hOaPWA)![](https://lh7-rt.googleusercontent.com/docsz/AD_4nXeCc27PvrTINwiF9gLz3V31iXM-p4nKJ9A5QtsdGN1eXhoiOUS7yIgZdCegHnB_hKvFX7pQ5QRMf3tpiMu9gTGy1Bmlspc53e_vO7JCFWX3GOwZzHCzL5LTYNQztMcUoPGpOgR6KYgYH7Lx5QiLnHF7TJFZ?key=rxGnIOzTXwvvF_Z1hOaPWA)  
This is the see IJ queue-based setup. It’s very similar to the see I setup for IOSZ.

![](https://lh7-rt.googleusercontent.com/docsz/AD_4nXecM9WEQJQ8YymkRGcf41AtoyL0moyfQixc6pttckSmyfcWLA6RnpS3jU7r6a3oLXzJGVUwaTP7g6tU74hGmDWNWtZpOsXW3OUZ_z91bzEZCZB9BERlIqXXAxEs0OYTV8Y3VksY3rGuBkXrJnlYhN4IOZE4?key=rxGnIOzTXwvvF_Z1hOaPWA)

This is the see IL queue-based setup. It’s about half-and-half save O/T.  
These setups cover about 85% of all queues, and are mostly what you’ll need. If they don’t apply, then you have a 94% chance to save T/O with this setup:  
![](https://lh7-rt.googleusercontent.com/docsz/AD_4nXcWuZizGmQmZ0aC1zbru4DKXaRV2eBYkItK0PPCjpgRnyFfQ_a3i_utC8a2XZwr4V1oZx5mLfJtZMKkf_95c3chV8nm0UzCXW4J_pG_zwfDwhAH3uJ9fm7t5J55fN1FVEnhnslnv7Ngv-2grvCZaN2zVC8p?key=rxGnIOzTXwvvF_Z1hOaPWA)  
It’s a setup that mirrors itself, so each of the ten solves has a counterpart, making it essentially five.

This will be a method with a little bit more strict queue-reading, with no real fallback setup.

Then, after this is where things start to fall off the deep end:  
![](https://lh7-rt.googleusercontent.com/docsz/AD_4nXecM9WEQJQ8YymkRGcf41AtoyL0moyfQixc6pttckSmyfcWLA6RnpS3jU7r6a3oLXzJGVUwaTP7g6tU74hGmDWNWtZpOsXW3OUZ_z91bzEZCZB9BERlIqXXAxEs0OYTV8Y3VksY3rGuBkXrJnlYhN4IOZE4?key=rxGnIOzTXwvvF_Z1hOaPWA)

We can borrow the see IL queue-based setup again, which is a saving grace, but then there are exactly two setups that are 100% save O/T on \[TLO]! and \[TIO]! queues.  
![](https://lh7-rt.googleusercontent.com/docsz/AD_4nXe8WtSzksydoIADfE-frMeyjtZgQvCN_E_lhZ6YoMNt4hK5MW_VeetaURavq9ZrTgD8r2cealPsgUFf0MG3BXHM8cUuaRtR8v-5pPBOMzs0L9EJho8mjAEgAgCpZoXwGuRt6LCGOUUfEL89o98lCjxaboCb?key=rxGnIOzTXwvvF_Z1hOaPWA)

This works for TLO. It’s the worst case setup, and the queue reading is incredibly hard to figure out.

![](https://lh7-rt.googleusercontent.com/docsz/AD_4nXcMqxK8Nu6NDUdhnL9nB6guoqy2kCcmBaPgM7BG4aFyzdbuS-vlPiiUhV6EzRB5Ivt_vaf0E0eXIvyXEMNs8xzils6k6wGMitfwqzw-iYHmmk1J3rGGK6Cky_hXPSzemi6AEEa4P30Lp5bRWzBZAcGb47iA?key=rxGnIOzTXwvvF_Z1hOaPWA)![](https://lh7-rt.googleusercontent.com/docsz/AD_4nXf4uksWoOZfUiscu4H3uf_kBBbGsO8GfdnG6XVp8XMlzxH-9JD1KFfuy30jbB0uztFanPQDCIVKJBQZVWWkrJ5POdCGZgwRTZJgM4sB_DWAO9SNWkTFbPHpDQXoPPHcHb_uQBPPOOPFsEfYVM_bMvx8whAN?key=rxGnIOzTXwvvF_Z1hOaPWA)![](https://lh7-rt.googleusercontent.com/docsz/AD_4nXc3n9xGkpYY-Xd-_iFlq074BqMMCC3Q8R2jqaurdpSqeAJpa00ltGWELF52zOyQuXtysnkPwjwXeAVxNY4D2lNejfeIkHwZkTojuLM0GfirNN0Mk1-x48OKaOzKs5-QqQMIrt9WkzNL8O2mTxkirKztJpBz?key=rxGnIOzTXwvvF_Z1hOaPWA)![](https://lh7-rt.googleusercontent.com/docsz/AD_4nXff9NzORcJMODLh1Z_QgPJO2k3GFEeNNeuUCnHE3TMonMspGGQeEEnMNtcVwNqlkHs_LN4US7JsLm2ErwXZgCie6MijnfP-Clu3wf4QUNF2rbndYcWify3CpBRrrS_mkqz46nBnZy59miEmye46U6I97pgf?key=rxGnIOzTXwvvF_Z1hOaPWA)![](https://lh7-rt.googleusercontent.com/docsz/AD_4nXcemRDYComMQKyy-JACDtKpnzeXiPesGPzeOzcH5fZ2rtrgw6SVwqlIlHjAbO1V8qFR_uj_GlU5s01umH6xOyDxUzgAp3eQ6g8vVOpyRgKGagc1HGStxgppvMcr0roL9mh6kvEIedjSN1Z6mvOLveefLw8?key=rxGnIOzTXwvvF_Z1hOaPWA)

Full queue reading:  
1st: I last, not J\<S\<Z // S last, not I\<J\<Z // Z last, S\<J\<I  
2nd: IS\<J  
3rd: Z last, J\<IS // I last, J\<S\<Z  
4th: Z last, I\<JS

5th: S last, I\<J\<Z

![](https://lh7-rt.googleusercontent.com/docsz/AD_4nXf7zxMMwic75i5yt-r0tpn-Tl_ySCIKbdliWsEsBDDI91i8pPE5JQee9JyVK1FtzXG9BOmtSWsW1IJjfeD8Bx89JxGqmCMB6JjS4_NN3q0-FHXkH7QtAunR3SO0OyVtnSNFiHK_HZ7xUTedYkq7sTtv2tCs?key=rxGnIOzTXwvvF_Z1hOaPWA)
![](https://lh7-rt.googleusercontent.com/docsz/AD_4nXdqj_-0KJJYKodXWyh4RNdCnCLA_sVXQnOB_dEOOVQYcilAmSGm5XQr-P3mmJuoAZ2duO9Y6Rtiv7er_FYuRikKKRv-0QZKtDzpMu1zzbrvz47XXGkuLqZFytCxD8jlQ8AyQBszcKcexIfiaRoZmwlaVikW?key=rxGnIOzTXwvvF_Z1hOaPWA)![](https://lh7-rt.googleusercontent.com/docsz/AD_4nXcf0zLxOrQ_L69SOW5SopGD4nCY-UiMnrf40K-Tsw-LiSqjeO50y2HZTKntC2mdxOuWgQm49vs8QxJyN7iphAU4zR4-ZbZEg3zLX6oM4J6Xi8lbwSXAZJGjUdvaxnVZwIzQvy4-J69kHnwXlItSKVrhnLoX?key=rxGnIOzTXwvvF_Z1hOaPWA)![](https://lh7-rt.googleusercontent.com/docsz/AD_4nXds5B4V2da49jAoWmq1-xVQ0FjhHzvgrSMlcGXkUlMAsW9ElloIWYF4abjcWESUvTnE_hQdruytAuXhC1x8exWRsXuutX7Ah91yZkYup8prjtuYfSS0wsAtQW4Nx1k4NfH8k7VjGo0ip-G0TYp-6jXkeBdh?key=rxGnIOzTXwvvF_Z1hOaPWA)![](https://lh7-rt.googleusercontent.com/docsz/AD_4nXdf8BK1GRdAoaUGUyD4BFNJStmuBXBSthLgMV47nR_wFtWk_aFQp6fkEep8h4NC2cjpYcltT4okICFWIViCyZLcfeYPq-JGssogwRbIDQBuL6abzagKHYCTffm2xEmUvPYOZTl8z0KZsKOpEeOwYIn7EZJC?key=rxGnIOzTXwvvF_Z1hOaPWA)  
The solves are in order:  
S last (upright S placed first) or S\<J (flat S placed first) 
L last
Z last, L\<S  
Z last, J\<S\<L
## TJLS/TJLZ 
TJLS is TIOS’s older and much more flexible sibling. It’s got the same two 70% cover S and Z queue-based setups, but it’s much nicer when those aren’t covered. The fallback setup I use can be used with the two S and Z queue-based solves about 90% of the time, but the moment you can’t use those solves, it quickly spirals out of control for the solution count.  
Reader beware, the setups get weird very quickly.

![](https://lh7-rt.googleusercontent.com/docsz/AD_4nXeLFA2jlgzXMHraJ0G3N6Ik2Zg2Fhy0UDEHpnAtYqwJJhjJQGRBMAq9hI490TqJTvNQ_wRibxmVIBGzaHbgSb-c88-hwVOjXGdHbsxvBUXPijgOe0VWlS7kTDNwtThv7sFODgQex3ltqA5UtYfwZLDWibF8?key=rxGnIOzTXwvvF_Z1hOaPWA)![](https://lh7-rt.googleusercontent.com/docsz/AD_4nXdqZgNqyed3n6AoQXcMG-UuQf5e5_Jc328lhgNoZo1rwjWt8iJM6Bql0LsC7m3Y2GkHCGCQdhN0Lb_NlcbikDoqg8WMefegg0q_tvuJbJ0snOxWb3PMC6HDLFb6lAHR1JwnREldBlnRZf8w2miFLhhRBeLz?key=rxGnIOzTXwvvF_Z1hOaPWA)![](https://lh7-rt.googleusercontent.com/docsz/AD_4nXfm4wwiWrmeHJJiXVtDK9MUbG8_pr90IC_ATGrs6LdElkOtRHX5UtFhZe_0tD3sXs1UXCyxqcHMYPSV4OOsHucdxJGQTMesEsBq--2PLoOtXZRI82nhORylxrBDYks85hmS_ds8j8DFunVJd970D0kuOEk?key=rxGnIOzTXwvvF_Z1hOaPWA)

These last four solutions may seem scary, but they’re for when J or L is last. The first two are for S/Z last, or S/Z before T or O.

### TJLS/TJLZ-alt

This is my personal method. I think it is better. But, I hope you realize how much bias is loaded in this statement.

# Odd JL, no T (not included)
All of Odd JL, no T cannot save T. Setups are very bad, and when T is last in the queue, you are forced to save either L or J, and the setup percentage drops heavily. Percent is what you focus on to increase, not saves. This document isn’t suited for that, so I’ve elected to omit them.  

See [this document](https://docs.google.com/document/d/1Py2PMJUjsv0yMtrnJxU1agmHjmwMnLF-OOQUBOvyW2Q/edit) for methods relating to them.
# Odd JL, with T
Almost all of Odd JL, with T is covered by two shapes: Tub and Heart + PCO.
## TIJO/TILO
TIJO can get a little weird for some queues, but it’s very versatile if you know what you’re doing. I’ve separated the method into Has S/Z and Doesn’t Have SZ. This is a no-fallback method, so it’s entirely queue-based.

Has S/Z represents five solves out of the full amount.

![](https://lh7-rt.googleusercontent.com/docsz/AD_4nXfjRTd5aweRT8R0_K3QeARFWM4I8RVdZI4BEbsa2fubV-CZfGUbFYROqtpOv5uS-LbuWT9iT3OAOreBCbwy5ABLYESQuBtoLmWHZPPPrkAhV8AtYfty0qhgiqVE9htlaNX38ANkl5wytnMv0CfDaQsUSOA?key=rxGnIOzTXwvvF_Z1hOaPWA)![](https://lh7-rt.googleusercontent.com/docsz/AD_4nXetguQVt5gxzLoutvpYcXYiL_bx-SrraqaCqIptXHlEwnlyq-SAuGCIIUxNxIcq6gsGU_nRPXMStVyoh9X1rdPXz_t2GpeFtpm9BCcEowsLk6XeyaHOhd2vNCQbliZY7p9VIhFKhwLQQBKHqfiAL2EFihvN?key=rxGnIOzTXwvvF_Z1hOaPWA)![](https://lh7-rt.googleusercontent.com/docsz/AD_4nXd2s9K0ZnmtDiChqKcvNpC66JBXEqHT-CYwj6fITsWBJrsCofesVbWUvCFuDchVWlmJOi6pGITucg7pdHbiRlN8fkZBuWgLushR--Ds4_4dBsJxj1wMrVqw-vigl5lIE4M0pxFhkCc_vqCOAOcd6Bj14iDD?key=rxGnIOzTXwvvF_Z1hOaPWA)  
See S, S before any two of \[OZT]. Saves O. Fails on a few other queues, but there’s always another save O setup.

![](https://lh7-rt.googleusercontent.com/docsz/AD_4nXcv8DYBKJ4i7HQwymddWc3OFZ_he1ujA2p6QudxTY1TKdk-903GcQzFzM198tMjzngrAepEnczeKooz_U5Nesup1kAp1VFYHFwT4AH1mIewQWviNn949FhYWQMHXEBhO33L9sVz3unjFQPZCyUSvftZEBgm?key=rxGnIOzTXwvvF_Z1hOaPWA)![](https://lh7-rt.googleusercontent.com/docsz/AD_4nXedQihbuLJAX9sIWgFMyJpcyTMYycMFlEHEQd_KbLPVwZ6ZNBe5x746-KhGQmUuRPW4WtrOnelw2YHuiQBdpSB_ofRvc4oVwTPS2c5TXuTWPxhpodijLa284MdVAKqiHJIB0gxJaMPIYowMaAvsfUfwNglx?key=rxGnIOzTXwvvF_Z1hOaPWA)![](https://lh7-rt.googleusercontent.com/docsz/AD_4nXecN_tEqx2rnKbUb3ZX9D1ZqgWsgL-jWfjThIO5RRi8QrhQZmhg_KVo1RliJ6WM8dBniWbr0yWHuQxhnQuKyUUPMYcJdMmL58qjDZF5_Vh1y9Gws_IeM6kZYp0_LnQgw259tCuFcy-JUtJTxXu3tef7vMoN?key=rxGnIOzTXwvvF_Z1hOaPWA)
See Z, Z before O and one of LS. Order is based on ST order. If you can’t build either of these when you see S or Z, the ST and OZ queue-based setups will work.  
![](https://lh7-rt.googleusercontent.com/docsz/AD_4nXebiLB1O6Uqiil1NDfqsVsfRwbNPV7CMiFErZosVBqlWQKpgikubZ1HjIjomSE87lwrgOG3BqYxNoWU4-mQ96DAUWWyzZ2mXUMa7vOXYQ0kFlwf5TuU-4QZ_5PMkXi76qc1JUG56jvaP6STB2cC8FBQ8Tbe?key=rxGnIOzTXwvvF_Z1hOaPWA)![](https://lh7-rt.googleusercontent.com/docsz/AD_4nXfa9GWNem9w5xvzSRT4PBCDQCuE30YRT7MpxFe8P3EKB6vfBAYSPshY7MxDdW25b-6_7WCPIPcTQKC-FF7rYLiMhHJhXM2tgGmvzSbkDP6iD1kP75XQVBMH9fusxBBilYP341-a07diIXx3h2xRy7CYatCn?key=rxGnIOzTXwvvF_Z1hOaPWA)![](https://lh7-rt.googleusercontent.com/docsz/AD_4nXc2lna7l-lRLTA7VR4b0T-GjgvTknWyIJyI9lFUeRRMnqEpbJ5urxOFZuXIacBlX4kULn2iBNdHhAB3wm7UdNW2kzux64qbKAq9f8vjFMhMkI3GkdZwGIgJHzh2yXzXN1fHIZTlr_NL8bzN4dp7MObV7mg?key=rxGnIOzTXwvvF_Z1hOaPWA)  
See OZ queue-based setup. Saves T. It’s just Heart + PCO, if you’re already familiarized.
![](https://lh7-rt.googleusercontent.com/docsz/AD_4nXeSPkUsSKBPcSaik4uowUiiFCSQQCbwOpIk2a-GwoWa-k864s9lpiIrEWP7Y749s6P-CUaRGJVPgnzmZxynQ6AeVkK8iBQIi_bIS69RwGQpPN03e1UHh6RBDWdRcAVX6WQ6Nwf_jwSUlsGCy3ZHWmKqAFM?key=rxGnIOzTXwvvF_Z1hOaPWA)![](https://lh7-rt.googleusercontent.com/docsz/AD_4nXdQ5WY4R6-O4-bCVOc3IEtWKJ_D6bhTAoquOcnGHOEMDZIf7zPbGAZGvzhm6qi5mhmx25tiX7qR60DoC_9pl38wK5C8rQkdlglBGNjSfkqVN1I3uSLun04SX4QLD72kniRv2vinivJd-UmWR-gRycglG0RF?key=rxGnIOzTXwvvF_Z1hOaPWA)![](https://lh7-rt.googleusercontent.com/docsz/AD_4nXcQhzCeig2Cl8c2gq3KY1kSWozW8O3FoSTBPmTcQzc48HcehAw8sNwrRQMrJ8tp6CXaa60rdtzCJyMeLlVruSVu-Kcx89VAqzvA9BGTsM1R-OnVRcHD_W7nJ43oG_LqRhvLNlHncBT6YnRy9OHbkj_gvS8d?key=rxGnIOzTXwvvF_Z1hOaPWA)
Doesn’t Have SZ represents nine out of the 14 solves.

## TIJS/TILZ 
TIJS is the easiest case out of all of these. It has a four-solve 100% O setup that also has 42% save T.

## TIJZ/TILS 
TIJZ can get rather uncomfortable for good setups, but it’s got reasonable queue-based setups to make up for it. Since Tub is not always buildable, I’m very specifically avoiding it. It’s why you see the normal Tub-related 100% O queues actually being given setups. Halfway through figuring out the fallback setup for this, I realized it would be much easier to just finish it with an entirely queue-based setup list.
![](https://lh7-rt.googleusercontent.com/docsz/AD_4nXccqyrTLE5PwwNJU67zbAV8jjZr5MDFfFT4YnPwGEJER9fzeAqQX7NFHgyBLPdrveYI4D94TpicbZp7lL4d2IJ8XIbJcXGTvdzkwRF03xjjglNDel0ClZQA2yRsrUIBBRblkYmAgaYzfq6rBxaZmK_bXwkS?key=rxGnIOzTXwvvF_Z1hOaPWA)![](https://lh7-rt.googleusercontent.com/docsz/AD_4nXcLIC4-ljF229986BXxBccJ9fzHcDULOy_jSShH6wi9723weOqW2Kfbn0Dt0UCLLr6J3CVY4yLZIX22to-YBhhMXdkVnNNgu1SUPlqQQ9TiTqpbvBm8oE1w6T0duvbVl-Uc6zp-H5PeOTwHOgzqSBXJxIUW?key=rxGnIOzTXwvvF_Z1hOaPWA)![](https://lh7-rt.googleusercontent.com/docsz/AD_4nXfjstYyG5E4dv6Lg0DwzlZ9eSPnuDV4Y4BWlFpXwxkh0jPze-_u7a_dulCaBlDrJ_nvQp7A33W6aiM7UcJ9fZiCZvGkP_iYeKWCKb2rGq9tr0579MIacER9eUhwJGiuL9atMRcmj09TjyntBYk--GW-PmOA?key=rxGnIOzTXwvvF_Z1hOaPWA)  
See T. Saves O. Straightforward.  
![](https://lh7-rt.googleusercontent.com/docsz/AD_4nXf6Bt6xsnEbX60PsU0ehXXFTttX5yeaPG6oep735H9hQDLDm83c_BQnLCIFGzNE3-1Np4U-aDUbw5RZs9Cf7aQFHK3bDyNZnyrvJdAyfel6zed9qFnGOg3JZHHZleSaRZfd9juXN4QPtuIb-v9h0tEWDpvv?key=rxGnIOzTXwvvF_Z1hOaPWA)![](https://lh7-rt.googleusercontent.com/docsz/AD_4nXfp2dZE5O1qSCG1SEDWNTprE6mwfMduaP1sKNUIENPrHAz5cGvICycjbU55gM5V8Nq3bXd11lte9DOXGxPhK2jEeTH9oMDf3_lHCnbQXbVCDJYn0KPlXv7tu7jxPgWS1dmUDcGWACe_k--6OrtrOz2zM8BL?key=rxGnIOzTXwvvF_Z1hOaPWA)![](https://lh7-rt.googleusercontent.com/docsz/AD_4nXetoxK2BgV8CJ7U4KceuTLDefKu-mb0fRow2lvXsTf-FpvofGaZgVqVzaw92Yhx6SjdtrJ9vlIZqo7bbMjDjwMQJjL21miigOeWjJ77AT0IE-V-v-tu3rQLCAbwIQ5d-8U1GqaaL5wmtZ62PuiwhTqa8v8r?key=rxGnIOzTXwvvF_Z1hOaPWA)![](https://lh7-rt.googleusercontent.com/docsz/AD_4nXeAZ7H_nCCjT6J4FC0LR-MxEt9OvzNAtU3moa8c3au7FWzDbll5bvSRBR1b9RpyTIwLiXH74DlTGfrBm_wRmKah-HS_QvlJPhmd_IxS8bHH2UKMK9q1wPtPvybPtcut3fojMSHsZfmqrPjcvX1Nx8JeR3x7?key=rxGnIOzTXwvvF_Z1hOaPWA)  
See S, two-solve save O setup. Fails on \[ZO]!S queues. First solve is J before T, second solve is T before J. If not, then these will work.  
![](https://lh7-rt.googleusercontent.com/docsz/AD_4nXe3J05DBoqo-4M1yGWwRte4CfpJTe8oVAxVgUkqfIkp1JvXKAoRsYnFgRx3wKLin8_BQxICF09yXoDYdYS2_lTmFe2WHUMX0sqxbaW5zd4b19DAS4AT4LBCNIPEu_70jl_beCQuO8e2eYB_UiEiXWJyyeU?key=rxGnIOzTXwvvF_Z1hOaPWA)![](https://lh7-rt.googleusercontent.com/docsz/AD_4nXcBydFp6VNeYsegOu-W14HatEt-F4y9FY2HzHUqHlJV0wBU1WOVY0-foME2dxkw4gMjh9z_KMGvgaAmhAn3r2lJX5Y2d-BaSaV6gcquZ7cgF9jDChWs-TnfVh2QJhqfWwsev4Ga-VOgkNhAAY-W-rjtRHIa?key=rxGnIOzTXwvvF_Z1hOaPWA)![](https://lh7-rt.googleusercontent.com/docsz/AD_4nXdXww_Lq2yHy-yQNzoScFD0GCNEl0bx5hlm3I0JaRsZrytPDcvnVhmPut8HQLnQsiz8LISzmyY47qlFEHdGYl6YhEuiWoNIGP-iUyeluH5N5yf5fv_D42rNcJaoJyQIs4Z6RmrTKtD2vDSva8CvapK1t0Y?key=rxGnIOzTXwvvF_Z1hOaPWA)  
See ZO queue-based setup. Saves T. It’s just Heart + PCO.

If none of the above setups work, then you are guaranteed to have at least one J/L in the queue. We can return to the same 3p with some different solves.  
![](https://lh7-rt.googleusercontent.com/docsz/AD_4nXehWbBNXl4vX0QW2R_3-EL2tn9hz328qCed2mg-m9AodMHRZdSd28SL5Wpbhs3o5myirsIE9sPiHOAqEQxznz3hYOWdg8141Q7w4A1qvp98l_-dhB11nI4qoIhFzCArMUL398rv76Ibigkgyd71a-dq_1bA?key=rxGnIOzTXwvvF_Z1hOaPWA)  
![](https://lh7-rt.googleusercontent.com/docsz/AD_4nXcF0__w0jOOQskZPly0Rsb0cuKOdzeXFO6dgpP7bZXKHeH_SXpXsu5o1kzH7HUw9t327jii4pbG6q_P6TDoPg0esIGHJ9u3xAln_rZdbxofsk0rWZwBzzUnDkQ8jX70fgMwk-X5j0fc_cHXHf86VNH0Ie4?key=rxGnIOzTXwvvF_Z1hOaPWA)![](https://lh7-rt.googleusercontent.com/docsz/AD_4nXeGcg2BxBBHz21rFUbioP3RJdEnOGQJkFdq24f5bag5RSCZYxHE1DG14wdx_qM_iW9HseV8jqOjPLM8szu1vHqcWGg9xpDdoUpdFjPCpW-kOVDVinprR5At5XO43fjIOu9I5HwvB77e6KVzgg0cJs3ZEdU?key=rxGnIOzTXwvvF_Z1hOaPWA)![](https://lh7-rt.googleusercontent.com/docsz/AD_4nXdKBVkbsPZT6Fi7BL-5vcvluHlZqm-W2YtUPPxI5y33343S_Inxc30wdZZr83KeF_Zj_CLuU1ASv4Ic_OFtYQIuoXow5x3LtoI-A-DYrjKaHRGr39HYcIcDmnmBjHM4QAPunTG_UAWACzLuKlnrxS0p1iU?key=rxGnIOzTXwvvF_Z1hOaPWA)![](https://lh7-rt.googleusercontent.com/docsz/AD_4nXe3ZnCQu_5k22DfgZh86J-xePgUyp8GFn6oCRocdX5F2vNCUKHTWQue79Q40BcY4VHf5MZV20arIZMQc4-tzUONgGM80CBcGmlmV9yiSwvkND2-49FlgVnNzfjOX6PtClTAIeZR_pwM3P5fPc4MUCL1vVqq?key=rxGnIOzTXwvvF_Z1hOaPWA)  
The first two solves are for when T is before S, and the other two are for when S is before T. Place T flat on JZ for the first two, place it horizontally on Z for the last two.
## TJOS/TLOZ*
TJOS does have one sort-of-simple high-cover queue-based setup, but it’s much more iffy than, say, the S or Z queue-based setups of TIOS. It’s still very high-cover though. It’s for see Z.  
![](https://lh7-rt.googleusercontent.com/docsz/AD_4nXfjglrb2qray1ArzOrA3CVrPK_eRqWwkndmVOAVrFAh8VU36IyKgkcC3iJD-FFN95b6ifCv_EZO58O0UiHR0U-M1HtC6pqbfgkZpjO3xmJDVK_CO9B3Jo1niHPCZJGbaDAh6lu08BFvGYDQurdfvezplGM?key=rxGnIOzTXwvvF_Z1hOaPWA)![](https://lh7-rt.googleusercontent.com/docsz/AD_4nXekIfcCrLgP1ehy1j_0YSCfcY1cL71pT8EBxYkVaX9dQ2EjChJ75Kf12D77RKmxudM68mu2vGGXpDr6Ukj9ZmUGQKnmL7RFNoAplixI18LcIbSsbWWlyanp_hZmxuvP_6bzFIQhP-8Gap9GMs-nEETNzig?key=rxGnIOzTXwvvF_Z1hOaPWA)![](https://lh7-rt.googleusercontent.com/docsz/AD_4nXfQK-oBhdfZkiTHN5TKYmqmYbSDDA2pp62ma_34ifDgEDyTP5X9GRxqTUL_NwH_hVmrebvrwrz7bI1l6ciC8NM_BNHJ1gS5-2O-4hXGpD2ZPE-5-xGscV6Off-CeZfgVVuZ9Zmf7Kt_4mmMlQDSFoRjG-Ck?key=rxGnIOzTXwvvF_Z1hOaPWA)![](https://lh7-rt.googleusercontent.com/docsz/AD_4nXdACLMrOk8ZZKBDWwAGApgY2NtoGXbgBOImr--qw3ApYcncy1zXTRYMkZB63rSD5gyDTRA4SMEu69cjooEBHSdK2sskUxdo4FUzOaHhA2XcIfvzm8HBkCx4I61lbrs-gHU3JrrNSvZjESIsLTlIjlyqhp8m?key=rxGnIOzTXwvvF_Z1hOaPWA)  
The first solution is for I before J. Second solution is for L before I, and the third is for J before I and L. Note how it’s incredibly similar to a 7th setup. (that’s now deprecated)  
This is the See Z queue-based setup. It does fail on queues with \[TZ]! in them, so use the next listed queue-based setup, which saves O.  
![](https://lh7-rt.googleusercontent.com/docsz/AD_4nXflCG2AOYrZcIVm1t0lohS4NHAwqYA4WpYDivtnmtXWfFrRo5hnpDLso64U-US0-XDKkQ1N-JfxUme3JbMgFjmpanNjYFBQjlcxqG9RKJNaN3yGE8H6Urfp4Dd_R-LeFULdTokcGD_KA-O1ABJ0Dr5AiHY?key=rxGnIOzTXwvvF_Z1hOaPWA)![](https://lh7-rt.googleusercontent.com/docsz/AD_4nXe3v10gaERmQLoZr3zCN9F_XUzJcL4XHXS1aW_StYqCkF4cmlK8Sy17bt7sFyjWH0lw8VIDZp5jK7VpPxNCpXlSSArs_f-8yeImyhMQBvAqrlJ3jqg80G9OgPtr0GCjwwudE_1q3XtnGB4NEAzUn36PMhdW?key=rxGnIOzTXwvvF_Z1hOaPWA)![](https://lh7-rt.googleusercontent.com/docsz/AD_4nXfg9V-X4jJAYjT0KEo6o3tbYvtJxHtPq1EHeL0LsaDCd9ORulLGvtLtgUjplYOy54XYfIE1D1LRZc6PaPHwJQdbBXZJ1KLQRsGTAUGOc9zRydF2Rrt3ewUhungq3szggKDh-Yvjet-azQ6n1NWfIra6RXZ7?key=rxGnIOzTXwvvF_Z1hOaPWA)  
As the above message states. See TZ setup, save O.  
![](https://lh7-rt.googleusercontent.com/docsz/AD_4nXdO0Nv1XjYQjC2LGqPFied3R9z7HnDoCPrXlvE_lfYmQGrVYRkFlFP-mdhwhe4P9udwTdwZnHeszr5HRWEXp4NyIS_yY0KjBUGd9bzeIePCx-L7VPynj5J5kkRuK1q0F2HKojFo00mYg1uJ7C6I7-1lpaqa?key=rxGnIOzTXwvvF_Z1hOaPWA)![](https://lh7-rt.googleusercontent.com/docsz/AD_4nXcgMf7RSzyQFtr3a7j7h-izmghO73L-ij2XqghzN7n7bFCwn9qV_lEUKStmS_L5AmoBr1LkQ_5_8LgcbKIQIpXpcpn0ShkMVD4TwxZyCqwroeVKpgF2xOG-xDP6M67HU5ZV4kmqkmZdS6u65Q92ZQrLykPo?key=rxGnIOzTXwvvF_Z1hOaPWA)![](https://lh7-rt.googleusercontent.com/docsz/AD_4nXeb2bKNcskLQ0H40E4h2Oq3EKiIQrJpq5FA5oDsmvk1apLge2OegMepx1zybYzlsG7jsX-6vAlJOW6LshX7Cn91wo8II3_z5m0sqJxAReZLhfsnnW1Ik1EGTFkhrreUyV1gbYQyJF8qCCbHZAQ2-bs-sdfa?key=rxGnIOzTXwvvF_Z1hOaPWA)  
See SO queue-based setup. It’s a modified version of Heart + PCO to make it 100% buildable.  
![](https://lh7-rt.googleusercontent.com/docsz/AD_4nXeikEQ_QEw6NNsF0OzLcnr2CBahKA2nIBT-zV35NGdI3VDt64_a_DsSz6g2cZuM0BZYqTMS8tjFk4gJSFkAliBTSQ0p_QfPHBaY-wwQ2f3qV7rO7kA9SB7_nSEpxFPKydIvQT6WM2Pn6lN_Z9noFNeASN_L?key=rxGnIOzTXwvvF_Z1hOaPWA)![](https://lh7-rt.googleusercontent.com/docsz/AD_4nXcV2e6gQZY-EqT86oEWueswV2jnUpXDDg2aRrzzcVVmIBH--X07EPM-WAptVvB10Fokim4TZ61o5Nob_WCtYKRDDBdyBOy6CuKsVTuzkNdLsH0L1RYTjGNwAP2uPV87V8CjJRa3GWeHzXxzX9XzY8-kjBs5?key=rxGnIOzTXwvvF_Z1hOaPWA)![](https://lh7-rt.googleusercontent.com/docsz/AD_4nXeTUaXNdMvTgLo2-S0eks0oT_4sD1D2q65jKZzOklKQY7qRa4km6U7DGaJ0un45UgSSboq5tfqO6beoYDYgYd2Lq5cgx1LB0w3JLWdhPyWtxvh8sMKV83SAbwxPG_WfuR4e9UGsdLHbbAu6-bq0uC3YJAM?key=rxGnIOzTXwvvF_Z1hOaPWA)  
![](https://lh7-rt.googleusercontent.com/docsz/AD_4nXdQQnAZqFuJPYwRh99wSl8KZnDLPhp8BOecNw1ajr7HTHNL-Gc3H9etzn1fqD8z1Rhjxgtp0gB6u8s25s4BuBn6js4paGC9-rrqupDWoi8ZOlvVjhFwYn6xTNuGBVN0UNxGGluNgaIsNSBR1db_fHR_5_B-?key=rxGnIOzTXwvvF_Z1hOaPWA)![](https://lh7-rt.googleusercontent.com/docsz/AD_4nXePvJ1cjC2UWYHW6U2WaCb9Z3P-YHFLqNoMQ9qMrk-qTXmsaaDnTEIMPGZU-co8gbXqWqkx6kvpoVmPxJJrtkSr2nSVGzx2c-GmRZtBBdZJjwASut3oEgXGJT1vcony3FJVDt1BPskPUgEVt8q6wRp7UAU?key=rxGnIOzTXwvvF_Z1hOaPWA)![](https://lh7-rt.googleusercontent.com/docsz/AD_4nXep-BF-thpBWNKrsImn5LBF2tHcqnrKYHH8uHSVH6t7--hIR3zB1lLO-B1Ltw_gag96ghy9n4DCHg2B057Rd39eaxYwgffL2qcOj1qd_3AfBhYkdARJ9zWHk-c5DbOCxcEam90t6Qe_Y7g6LifwrAzAUYg?key=rxGnIOzTXwvvF_Z1hOaPWA)  
Throwback from IJOT! See TL and TJ queue-based setups. These are to mitigate fail queues on the fallback setup.

For an inexplicably stupid reason, IOJ queues are god-awful for queue-based setups for TJOS. I lucked into a single reasonable setup.  
![](https://lh7-rt.googleusercontent.com/docsz/AD_4nXfej229wRK3slustfAu_nFaNi9r20uKZlYctJy-DHo9fmDatKuyBI9vcgGGFQQIMHmPYoDkalkshkluCTZ2g3B7I3r0PN2hlaFpcg3F0kdHpxvFt8AQvL5kE7GsjUkMobxtNJO_lyCrFFAtY8XcDiRzcUI?key=rxGnIOzTXwvvF_Z1hOaPWA)

For the last solve, you will have to change which T you place based on the order of TZ, where the on-S placement is for Z>T, and the floor placement is for T>Z.

Then, you can finally move onto the fallback setup, which, again, only fails on \[TOI]! queues.

Queue reading is based off of last piece: Z, S, L, and J last, respectively.
## TJOS/TLOZ (T/I)
TJOS T/I method is much, much easier than the T/O method. Mix a 7th PC setup with some save I solves, then shift it over when a spin doesn’t work.  
![](https://lh7-rt.googleusercontent.com/docsz/AD_4nXevYO9NyVU6D1G8_GwqLqbO3_kB-r6TlSlP8e9Utgt9FFrYEjVoItNqvT8acKelN-D5qTam-aN_G1VjuQUfmhf9zTzHoFv80tJ2T3i2v5mdIE_YP30xVv1sGr9qAKha-wCbIcRMeCYQxQJlORp1xJsKOCTS?key=rxGnIOzTXwvvF_Z1hOaPWA)

![](https://lh7-rt.googleusercontent.com/docsz/AD_4nXfVQs1UJVnoRBEP1xCttOeOGHzfVFjUu3XWiCvEHEA5FLchXtpKuiDDRs9JZ_vcSQKjVDrp1R-16r_uQ-wh-hzAsfof8DP755-CdTxlB2AZq8HCvPynCcEJLPEa61liCEl7Wg2pDSaSsrcRbCEHHlxf-a-Z?key=rxGnIOzTXwvvF_Z1hOaPWA)![](https://lh7-rt.googleusercontent.com/docsz/AD_4nXeAt2J6MfCOio4j7Oc03REr2ly9gWR7G7JrOPScQcZsFHDoZtOcldePgjKKbtORIK9noUeNEh8FZOEB8F4GX9Nw7OhWp-q_dEg4apQUOBOQcPS7-pREpUb5FHghlkPJHGCS2aONhbNnwyT5uMnzYNMhKdv5?key=rxGnIOzTXwvvF_Z1hOaPWA)![](https://lh7-rt.googleusercontent.com/docsz/AD_4nXeeE09p6SzAnt-dQfRAuE2Xys5C5T8KLmNpAZ_jI-clsLYLkLMPOXXZ93_Ea8BxEHMk0v1KOfytkEdK2atCiyftScMX3AO3aVdtY4rWikRqCCbR7F6zy56L57KdUzSRsmcDnlIg7cxEgXaldHWYvtymSk9F?key=rxGnIOzTXwvvF_Z1hOaPWA)![](https://lh7-rt.googleusercontent.com/docsz/AD_4nXcGFXgTS9yzLv6Z4af3NC7kWH84Q1GEu_38zlr-tRA-qk378TrRCm0jR9NnGq9udmze37kLxsjrQ-qrR68diEdqHxp3NNk8lA7YiMVKCH_ZzHWuIvxCtudNEGZIOSi-MNusyiZqRMyzqXd5vKBxy0VqflZx?key=rxGnIOzTXwvvF_Z1hOaPWA)![](https://lh7-rt.googleusercontent.com/docsz/AD_4nXd4ne-KDngLbB-4bQPutQeGqOKYZR_-g19aZGDbxw0cxufdYtrRtV7J_Ypl9q7gmkZxVVjaCdH0U4IJfhBpFjnJjXIUbVHfjCIPun-au0pVFScuMVkmGgxWAvmzy11ghnR94QpabdMkYJL-L_QM6zL2EC0?key=rxGnIOzTXwvvF_Z1hOaPWA)![](https://lh7-rt.googleusercontent.com/docsz/AD_4nXfrSWLcPHPKJddh2TH_uirQXC0RqSpwyB4OFmWqUpjiW-1sAY6KUIvcS1t5TtLP2S4DZFkB48Czqv1B2fzH5qdMmGH0fPOKwfsJO7CW27wrCIDO6of2MfEpYVMEv0IrHD8LOdOAXZjByy5fQnaGVTGklZg?key=rxGnIOzTXwvvF_Z1hOaPWA)  
The general queue reading I use is that the first four solves are for when Z is before T, and the next two are for otherwise. The last solve has a tricky J before L dependency, if you didn’t notice. That’s why it’s not entirely 100% T/I - it fails on ILS and ILJ queues.  
![](https://lh7-rt.googleusercontent.com/docsz/AD_4nXd1Mdv87z7R7Qn6IVnoiUTP4GiSBfFTgZ0pcJViPG_QCKmZVi_W7ckf1yq4EUdBXuIcjdqHMlU9Wmbz7hdcZP9NEq7l8nu5DYTheJ-0L5gjY774UBHsuOCP_TXnRs6u2Y2nFlAdenhNifCC7rEs9cR2stM?key=rxGnIOzTXwvvF_Z1hOaPWA)![](https://lh7-rt.googleusercontent.com/docsz/AD_4nXe_FfNQ0yeDmWNfQZXJ8K9DklUsZ5AtCoueV-3fy93UkOV1S6uKyc80hBiczYLa6g5aZrz7ZzUEqv3plG3i1Uwt-bzr_tCThBot7b0ZTINt-KmvT8b7tHOoMBnAnRDAQpVBqg5XjIZoNzVxXDBVLP6qA1pl?key=rxGnIOzTXwvvF_Z1hOaPWA)![](https://lh7-rt.googleusercontent.com/docsz/AD_4nXfCuUAagFlHigSW2b_F70SI2cX9-PVuXntkYk9F5RO45AuXptaXQVFf1rav2FoPeJbycaFFpoS6PT42OwDtDo9k7dezl1ZbCfFzQ6An46dQGCln8kom-CCkVBRl4NT7OLPLzJcvx_yQ9Y4yhO3qudmX18M?key=rxGnIOzTXwvvF_Z1hOaPWA)  
In that case, this will work as a general L queue-based setup. It’s shifted over so that the L has enough blocks to kick off of and can spin into the hole. Z before T, T before Z.
## TJOZ/TLOS
TJOZ is by far the worst non-dupe 2nd with T. The pieces hate each other with a passion, and it took a very large amount of blood, sweat and tears to refine a feasable method for 100% O/T. ![](https://lh7-rt.googleusercontent.com/docsz/AD_4nXdv-Dswvh_Hiij8GBpj0-MdXEUe8WA_ryl877trwIwLps0cbK-a2lmMD4xg7I5Y8u3YSaLriMfCF0hFKH0EQwtNXfsiTXd0FXRZm5jllE45Vvvnf92sKg4Qj91ajw1WN8d-2Dc_OF5PckZ2SxmKnQLPIuY?key=rxGnIOzTXwvvF_Z1hOaPWA)

![](https://lh7-rt.googleusercontent.com/docsz/AD_4nXcuDbaE-bgIr-Rk2_fYr1V2An7z6Sv833yozMPfWv3nSKzAsX5oIB6tfw-ggWzSSEwhyJQaUAjB9fuOQgNh7mnyC2NC2jqF1pKdgefqW4-G0A3KKmxIyYfkT8rFJ3iwfaJEndeHxymp-nkPNiRlrkAvRnpB?key=rxGnIOzTXwvvF_Z1hOaPWA)![](https://lh7-rt.googleusercontent.com/docsz/AD_4nXfA_J_l1RmVcHkUPkjpVgIrpCuS3sFGiGB9VZx4Wksf7srACvk65qyKNjc0GpMbvczmk-qToHCl_RfvG_Mslz4eZXzJD0Flu8uMsVQ5A99iik8NrTxzfx06jtQdVkVW8GSSBZewGFrjFeymBxdD06MqCNc?key=rxGnIOzTXwvvF_Z1hOaPWA)![](https://lh7-rt.googleusercontent.com/docsz/AD_4nXep5_kwuEZpCHGN1dIyGz9ks2AMNz2yzHRoGz9gUekOxFcEv3srqUp12kfx3-n08DiPp0FRNLrgUPoDyZ06b5qA3Z3d-Yya8pPnmqiyhZ3M2D-Yq0L-3Z6WZgTaKk_x3kIfjNmr-se6wqD6A0Ygk4Bzb2o?key=rxGnIOzTXwvvF_Z1hOaPWA)![](https://lh7-rt.googleusercontent.com/docsz/AD_4nXcu8zq0hmlNlazmGfQY3kQJ7B7s2ROgNi5IW9sPbgvSvGLHrpI44U992NgcHM8V9ZHv-agcMnDk0KBZwaTDfctqOcfce3KnIdPUCj-BKykbsG6EUN09K7hXPQ6HU3PxfgI8BUCry6BkzM39KbPCzQbfJFAV?key=rxGnIOzTXwvvF_Z1hOaPWA)

## TJSZ/TLSZ 

TJSZ has a few high-cover queue-based setups, and has Tub with a reasonable fallback. It gets rather complicated when you get bad queues, though.

![](https://lh7-rt.googleusercontent.com/docsz/AD_4nXf-TAIsHJi9u4riLuqBdnUOIk0j3rvfwRH79U_4qh-mLo80WMZx559nb6ZCqBI6wxPfLoenxFjWxaPLH7t9YWmdDx5Ayk6B-57gzyx6IUcYviAZFzguND1hbpWC0HeuSq5OXdU2lQXsZ2Qaai-lpQL-e6U?key=rxGnIOzTXwvvF_Z1hOaPWA)![](https://lh7-rt.googleusercontent.com/docsz/AD_4nXeBB2qiaIj_hyqIRUx5vwQO-wz4xKtbtPy6_1K_zc9KraMIfXSr7yjwsStvnGfemhxfr0XSZ0GM99-MJMftmkIRgMLPThuCLQ3byo-0VCF9d7fhWIguFrpcOlNBt-G4USXFVJ7DVF4Ynx-hc1Pw8iI5qBPq?key=rxGnIOzTXwvvF_Z1hOaPWA)![](https://lh7-rt.googleusercontent.com/docsz/AD_4nXfP6h2AAI37-MrOzuZvHMj9uIx0T_rrbc7iPM4l2BxC1h4tp4h7xk9m09dId9VYPSipJR4DCsJg6An9qsD4VY67yCe4ApcgNX9er_l34gp6svHGMGzB5g8xP8Ln_7zn1BLDYfZ59Ko8LfqBZdbD8xxBi8-e?key=rxGnIOzTXwvvF_Z1hOaPWA)  
See L, L before I or O. Saves O. Fails to be built on [IO]!,L queues, where Tub is 100% save O.  
![](https://lh7-rt.googleusercontent.com/docsz/AD_4nXfgb48SHjQwg9WxwgXsYgVT6E2Wgxt_ZcJhtel77iLk7b1ytdPP77xYZRaw5_X1nmmtKOISeeytMOx1a76cg1eoKFECccQUNoVry7Gt4BnrBgtVyAja0EKomzaSr0ON_3qj5kYZgET5ifZzmhiGYdZqrOY?key=rxGnIOzTXwvvF_Z1hOaPWA)![](https://lh7-rt.googleusercontent.com/docsz/AD_4nXd0G96UB3GLVohBi5UNbEhczyhkX1-bLbDZK4mScd6W-l3q7sfW6MOzUIhZpwXSoBxhWng2xhy2Ap7lU_vw4d8hEhy4ClmWT6Q9NvhLZRjKsvmRMGsvOvp2LEC_zvpXaYb4Z4JOVjVk6ix0x4T-7PYMlnhq?key=rxGnIOzTXwvvF_Z1hOaPWA)![](https://lh7-rt.googleusercontent.com/docsz/AD_4nXeB3SHZHfruyVayMlSnP78MZb3w2TPPGnCgGZSuwrbnfh4ozFdWrWHrTeGhPZ50H26QZqSkXeljBnubOiScAeMGicE2HUOReA1w1OF3ykAKOxew9rBtG3bqDvIVYmiVVssdtFMQgWP8jLPIUhRT_x5a4PU?key=rxGnIOzTXwvvF_Z1hOaPWA)

See T, T before S or O. Saves O. Fails to be built on [SO]!,T queues, where there is a save T setup.

![](https://lh7-rt.googleusercontent.com/docsz/AD_4nXfZmKzFmkNMXef4VJI2yrRGoVGTfFXwEbwyIjnnuWBtBzgkyfgtku2bO9XakTjBzuqk1TefmQsJVLS7HN1yQVMnXBrTLu4puuOM89EMtg7M4BGD32lngeG6JBtzkt7d38niyjOcIVtF6v8R-OmLxtZ9BC7-?key=rxGnIOzTXwvvF_Z1hOaPWA)![](https://lh7-rt.googleusercontent.com/docsz/AD_4nXdltZxcZsPTGUTuOPBK6gOIjD4jZd3uz0f-2yzHP7AwQ9MiHAgQUl4vZO2Wk0mya8C4n8dW_hVg3q7cxTMQafvQw9JeShRLWQS4l4TeqG_YL0hyTWlBAcXyC-j9gZifmRMTLXIZKVHqA6o-n3dV2IeWLBWG?key=rxGnIOzTXwvvF_Z1hOaPWA)![](https://lh7-rt.googleusercontent.com/docsz/AD_4nXfjH-gYrQadKML7Xe19S2F0_B9r-YFG18wUWpv_nbIEm_cWhKbfuzDYl9hXO1WLpvrev3MY21F8-19hCjiiJpMnwYWrM-0WHVSJ4K1lwpRZcTqWh1Y0NrMkp6PsdqKODKzvlKbssA0ksn1zj6BJ9qnJkiwX?key=rxGnIOzTXwvvF_Z1hOaPWA)  
See SO queue-based setup. Saves T, instead. It’s one of two T saves in this set.  
![](https://lh7-rt.googleusercontent.com/docsz/AD_4nXc-8Y14LToZ6h5Yt5pYWWEX29nI4wrP8vtCjx0d60EwIVjfBI6-ieRG1s2tVMJjz38aPAduzaJJ5eY2UqCid8vb9I7jhHG8wxp5GYiwEqOUqfds_PIiGhDAiv22SWaToHcrhYpwP8_uYiGgXSoYvXIysW4?key=rxGnIOzTXwvvF_Z1hOaPWA)![](https://lh7-rt.googleusercontent.com/docsz/AD_4nXfWWtltUjO9y_MzPRLG8xEqTpRCRPT8YuirP3ztB4S2jqX6KcpdbIvGjDbuDX6GlEYJuN-lcny6TGjw1ZePAgfBGLTbX8_hL0CPdI9KE-1I7WxlrML6g4EgTMhbJQeHH1WgeYPJRPYnmsxITBq7zOBkRsNp?key=rxGnIOzTXwvvF_Z1hOaPWA)![](https://lh7-rt.googleusercontent.com/docsz/AD_4nXeAG9tkqPHErASw2dJtKKg3ThSKI6c5SU3jnS1EpoLjBhdgZKa-l_r5xWd2i10-hJig8Lvi7E0S-E6mXGtYqCOAoKi2mNrTVLwM9IWMcrUihYFEIs-U8GO-UUVJ0NHO99Sp6UpHlHr5vqw530GGXBE-Dr0?key=rxGnIOzTXwvvF_Z1hOaPWA)  
See IZ queue-based setup. Saves O.

While making this set, I managed to let queues like [JO]!I slip through. There is one four-piece setup that you can do to remedy these queues, but you might be better off ignoring them.

![](https://lh7-rt.googleusercontent.com/docsz/AD_4nXeKHU5qVa3Y-8StekUT9jWRRvaOo8xo-66BcH8fC-ufnJSonPuUEzkAkivqsweT-hE-pV8ID6oCEPCWFTAgkAXUY5QKZNQpxqe0BQrQetdL2zcuk5ZCXr3kRbMN5CCY_2yl570pi6G-TxC24co2HEV3tFg?key=rxGnIOzTXwvvF_Z1hOaPWA)

![](https://lh7-rt.googleusercontent.com/docsz/AD_4nXfQ6k7swiCcXzR88qL3ld5xFQtDZgSHhQrlt-_q56KqPZbHX77oK6CDVd0vMdQ08nkZxeD9dxE3m-9TQMCmwwF_qZUkzWp3va1kqZuI6c2QjAvTa5xMzKsTNH1H2wi68c9WH4Nrqfq0KYADz81sOc_eaCXy?key=rxGnIOzTXwvvF_Z1hOaPWA)![](https://lh7-rt.googleusercontent.com/docsz/AD_4nXeLZ26T1KgsUVIKZRf9V4GeSkGnXvHCOmisR0fHaiNtgiQ04hNvs0N0bg-61-Czi1LUpRXc7Q4qtqyyu9TcO7Illmf5zcsO9tZ-29chtG7u31ICKx9Bsd8rdfAyDbE1z7XBpaI3nkcIltaUgPz4nUZXrzM?key=rxGnIOzTXwvvF_Z1hOaPWA)![](https://lh7-rt.googleusercontent.com/docsz/AD_4nXfocvC-rGXRyS0vvW78m_YpWEE0gn1KH3-qkKiOX-8QTtW378XWhnjHIgGMEq4bg4rsZsCELokpBYn5oy98g_Bb1QYz68U_6eB-FspsPtacZiKDbmI7BJ5S7LXTs7vdAcdIq0X6SrD7O82uRmICERYHr7g?key=rxGnIOzTXwvvF_Z1hOaPWA)![](https://lh7-rt.googleusercontent.com/docsz/AD_4nXddJK-WTzp170QN63Bn5BkXgHTd9aH1hEI0F9ig2lFU1UCvHAIbGZjO3jRMAJVNlplJBItoz_DSEQ9yr3Q5DFme0A9n094lKDhQfK3YIuoMZj0Cz-ATR3C07i2rviCm5GnDRVh9IYSkYq3c-fE6JGFNDPM7?key=rxGnIOzTXwvvF_Z1hOaPWA)

In order, the solves are for L, S, T, or Z last. 

At this point, you’re only left with queues with either an L and an I, or \[LSZ]! queues. Tub is two solves for these queues, with solves being based off of JZ order.

![](https://lh7-rt.googleusercontent.com/docsz/AD_4nXfRsb7PhteFCgfhK1wtqD8aZ4wUHw4s7-a_kzlDHYkDHKqKLWkIBzUyxkmNMmCS5mMSgkKQ0YmF5KZOBaaIieaN7zn3ZrMeEiJsiEiCzPwZgYbTFHKpJjKapXmbCTgj2IqqR4k_FOQs2tt-RxA870Yq0-s5?key=rxGnIOzTXwvvF_Z1hOaPWA)

# Other Necessary Dupes
## JLOO
JLOO is a forced dupe queue from Jaws and IJLS box.

It’s incredibly unforgiving to any queue-based setups due to its bag composition, but it has a 16-solve 100% O/T setup, and that is about it. Luckily, a few of the solves are mirrors of each other.

## TSSZ/TSZZ
TSSZ/TSZZ is reachable from O\[SZ] 5th 2L.  
TSSZ is somehow better than some non-dupe with-T 2nd PCs (Looking at you, TJOZ) and has a one-piece save-O queue-based setup.

![](https://lh7-rt.googleusercontent.com/docsz/AD_4nXfpMK0shIggGx_vh6FwdMDhrdou2_UWYNFjj5o89YlXcSOgWQDOzx0rSfeYJmf9og1t--Kd6hYy3VLbLZIoo6e6vTJ7ie6nVd6cpM3QX-wqI4eSzeafIhSMYbGjwJNPTJvEl0JC-5yUBgOI1x5BnzeR_plW?key=rxGnIOzTXwvvF_Z1hOaPWA)![](https://lh7-rt.googleusercontent.com/docsz/AD_4nXfBi1xdYB3G-FZZi0CGA5u4Bv0mqAOngHbkoUdIVo03J5r_ObCXs0DhyXtdXWZLHDePan0n5Gu8PVgWlp6fl9K6nn2Twrg1l3fl0zILp_IgrxbkMbF1YbhBmSMB7DKwehsk0fHrtmWYKcSwYGOdsp2BirFj?key=rxGnIOzTXwvvF_Z1hOaPWA)![](https://lh7-rt.googleusercontent.com/docsz/AD_4nXdSmCSKWM4aGVYo_JgR3wgRpQofBcCU-7ErG8On0BCGi5O6AfXJj5yvHxaAAyr_xzrnbM7TKd8Q3Ve2RJdyBDuDAZGoQayG7gTppD6ttB636F7YRvD67Osj3Oz0kcDlkzbtCcT8abzVWUaxyVdxXmilp5o?key=rxGnIOzTXwvvF_Z1hOaPWA)
This is the see T queue-based setup. It’s incredibly easy to remember.
![](https://lh7-rt.googleusercontent.com/docsz/AD_4nXeB7hjF8yCWMlkQ2BzeypoDE9Rkr65WGE1k6KS5P12uMXXkfgrsXve1a-9oMI1kv60MuTZS57XDVgrzYsk6isEMKYZJwNAQ7qNdsy-cR_sqAGj5PcGe7W5BnkfBu8NomeK_Hylxy-xuqrzl4IY-0_tLEc0?key=rxGnIOzTXwvvF_Z1hOaPWA)![](https://lh7-rt.googleusercontent.com/docsz/AD_4nXchc1xHcq-kvCKQuHNLWGczgXxAQYxzutVyNNSo9gXRotYJuE7l69ldQBRzJ2xco5Spfyjd1-S99sXoGVH-_kBq6Vi8O50cuPiyVeJsCTq_o-WyG4KUFdDZLtgNSJ1LyscyHoW83f8A2eXj6rS3KLibbsB-?key=rxGnIOzTXwvvF_Z1hOaPWA)![](https://lh7-rt.googleusercontent.com/docsz/AD_4nXef2G73mSgCrNgSk7P3RcuyEu5IP2t8AgxMYXrGh2hWrp3EcmZYRYPvf7n6KAsy3rlDgv-CAQF1Py-ysTiDyLRZO64hWbfuSjlT8GbADc9E0NtwxGsIumKmm211CYRnVXPXUWKYR5Pnns8J29ALfIC1a6TT?key=rxGnIOzTXwvvF_Z1hOaPWA)
This is the JO save T queue-based setup. It’s rather similar to IOSZ’s JO save T setup. It fails on \[TJ]!,O and \[IJ]!,O queues, where either the T setup or the IJO queue-based setup can be built, which is directly next.

![](https://lh7-rt.googleusercontent.com/docsz/AD_4nXdAWi6H0ElsiOvgW8LceocuTExeVTARHdBku1gDOg-emdL1JArwJ2nKiNzXuGjLXGyiuP2ldqZo45WnYhV_DBBJeeCo2UBXcL0eAmI52syKuNGN5riFeXXfU94SIQy_HgSGuY_7xgMeCvks79l2oh2Ert0?key=rxGnIOzTXwvvF_Z1hOaPWA)![](https://lh7-rt.googleusercontent.com/docsz/AD_4nXcpIGKQjABTMHSWJUshC68_qh0D6ptx9om1Kyo8rsODrgFzV7lyQyp7-LMD3z-aL3lzJV5okBdUwDqTeMgsorh72BVly8n_ua-GIMh6kyErAWDEEeSKCGhSy9JYuFa1nls3x5aUpGCkoIbhoFBR9MqUDBM9?key=rxGnIOzTXwvvF_Z1hOaPWA)![](https://lh7-rt.googleusercontent.com/docsz/AD_4nXfCjk2ePrNo4ioXWmoc4fY4Ad1FsvAfRGkJ3HMmgj5_0006Y9xfZYN45ASZbFpmEEfs07Z60Y2cMNb_YEuqATM0BamFytnd8Bk3qJ0Y4CMLNgDkbpfc_2A-pWc52IyhhVWjgwLjmyOgceVJLKzjBVtyTa9m?key=rxGnIOzTXwvvF_Z1hOaPWA)
This is the aforementioned IJO queue-based setup. It’s rather similar to TSZ 7th.

![](https://lh7-rt.googleusercontent.com/docsz/AD_4nXdkyrXee7I-jxppoUusUkKrUhiRMQ_ZEgl4hKiNMCKKV8IrQsgrc43XZe2luvuAVtIA1T6zYN5OS2SmaUNOMDKOMSyXfmQt_vA_FLoTqFVpAZra4UQI1LWPgWTS725wOPZmdltbVoISmBwtAGU9fOVnXBXH?key=rxGnIOzTXwvvF_Z1hOaPWA)![](https://lh7-rt.googleusercontent.com/docsz/AD_4nXfivgLwWm_gxaJJuLV-XR05ByIrjVM-HWnC1lHFPO3DIOpLbPwunuyqBugyeLPGsgAdc_cZxcJEZoReqkvuHqYAsvZMDUvtO0GM-SHI-DuLmI-ShCThIaPqjGNfDSVbXptRqaMvC0zfnv8eus2567W52hSz?key=rxGnIOzTXwvvF_Z1hOaPWA)![](https://lh7-rt.googleusercontent.com/docsz/AD_4nXejC48CC9dL1RQggAFfXGdDZ-cDsVU3Ort8N7bdCJ1XoEhHcI8BdbGyyW6Hvq83GmHK1njmKpamY6vYpCCdLfI1fqHkWprnfOzi-qP3DxbfBMjDivF544mpXUvPJ6lgQlIVDcdn9QJ1m-RFd5mCKV-JQUrL?key=rxGnIOzTXwvvF_Z1hOaPWA)
This is the LO queue-based setup. It’s very similar to the JO save T setup, and it fails on the same queues, so there also has to be an \[IL]!,O setup for when you can’t build it.  
![](https://lh7-rt.googleusercontent.com/docsz/AD_4nXccXhVdWzFmZ9qwimJRAAvMDetjWmVoAyLTb5sRezJ9aQ0ay7xoyQTdm_xX8NTXMwbjDnOekLYMO_Ipi0I7pHiUrGWkHA_DXeugau_84OoMNQGwWaaA4boVyKg0OcTftFOTYdpE3dpk1XRdWz2m2M4LMuLp?key=rxGnIOzTXwvvF_Z1hOaPWA)![](https://lh7-rt.googleusercontent.com/docsz/AD_4nXdeqm_CrHH0Kb_PaCpEPmtHkvc9grBO8Lnr0knaIrZPAeNbmacKxtPur6iBLwluekAT4UrhwKkvjmsqgAr8mFAa4ekqJeLo--nqPUzWizGfBKww4O5bVHouxB4WmUlajg0awesAo8qxtJRC9FwueJ9KkeA?key=rxGnIOzTXwvvF_Z1hOaPWA)![](https://lh7-rt.googleusercontent.com/docsz/AD_4nXeupWJAhFWiCJVZn-vvMuNpClW2svKLDCuDoMvvJI72dncHLAdkrroPUqwUo4Mwdc6vPeEkm_MidQmgGCMh2l61R2G7sgps7KgiU2xZlaDCBehq15VtEL_aVLlLpmP8uqMkCvgA7zY2e5UkFREVDhMdnLU?key=rxGnIOzTXwvvF_Z1hOaPWA)  
This is a slightly different, and less-covering ILO queue-based setup for the fail queues on the LO queue-based setup.

![](https://lh7-rt.googleusercontent.com/docsz/AD_4nXejz2mJde59bHhJTShWaGOaFOy8hEjcDXbkER1pASXYora_gx4-nXkVvmTlLsgAJ5be1wGYkP0O0pULlfED0P4gkvR2ptRq61Mp72AyV_kMhitLAyZ_crnJvaKK8DINeIi251or_1VenW71EaayUytRFJsk?key=rxGnIOzTXwvvF_Z1hOaPWA)![](https://lh7-rt.googleusercontent.com/docsz/AD_4nXclgeUS4TAoYhj6IpLgGN7Rblz5MHRF1pLvQbgbi7GDqCOGwdsxhTDjNMKYw0j-5q3eieRhfn6sSt-PqZnAW5j6fPEkFcfhy50HAqE6ok30LFSmoFnTSO0iXSdEHz7IzYkJkhbwcRKOrZdvsfKl3jENvI3V?key=rxGnIOzTXwvvF_Z1hOaPWA)![](https://lh7-rt.googleusercontent.com/docsz/AD_4nXejvH7Pj0XD4XSOWbCVQS_dRIlFzHDSOsy-wll9hNbkHrFEO1mjEFQU73qIn6QkWJGamsY-TiLvVxEbKj283O_q1cDtoBv022zN-gpG9H66rethxcrqJDmQI8MAvCNQTwEDeGv14Aj9KRGLLgyDTkHNIM3G?key=rxGnIOzTXwvvF_Z1hOaPWA)
Then, there is the IZ save O queue-based setup. It’s one of the more necessary setups, as \[IZO]! queues are a plague for Pepper.
![](https://lh7-rt.googleusercontent.com/docsz/AD_4nXfyn4ugaBxeOG2QhHCdyiL65qbThM401HC_pshRBnDrwGHF50WBBbmeK9LacIob-xZ1pGoGA5RAbL8H4OFVEWN9yLgi1uvuMpKhxO6zQZe6Spta0qqFpEfmDKzSZB0InCQRLlN2N9RewOaiIrkUzKlxLuaT?key=rxGnIOzTXwvvF_Z1hOaPWA)![](https://lh7-rt.googleusercontent.com/docsz/AD_4nXfjWroa2ytBcABv62KRG0JUBz-8E7gWRVMLLhsWyHM4evq25nkxJ8uNoQLs3xkVKL9MDBHMd8RmN_Or0UtRiSBUXlAaEu1jUz9vlmTAC0HVSdmoY3IgdRzGuOCIiKvQAavVrpLnRaoU_8npOq1U2xg8DpL6?key=rxGnIOzTXwvvF_Z1hOaPWA)![](https://lh7-rt.googleusercontent.com/docsz/AD_4nXch4sgU0idoJiv7eqHCU0JpaWE_0A9cgJtJBHUXxM-zcZoEgS36bDcB-jNrN-CND2MNzDSQGzdDvjE9I4Bhz2BCzKF8zpXrsnfWDBwm-GZ3rD0DxZkvPogB25yLw3M1xp4lCHc71xrCD9tl8wz_y1bTFEk?key=rxGnIOzTXwvvF_Z1hOaPWA)
The last queue-based setup you need is the ILJ queue-based setup, but it’s rarely needed.

Then, Pepper will be 100% O/T with 7 solves.  
![](https://lh7-rt.googleusercontent.com/docsz/AD_4nXfE27i52ODCqf2OojAfkCudJrg2qqaFgQw2gqQa6tsYXzz1n_M5J8MGbWdshM5UrUJC8V2v3ATaevVJCQd_OXHuwqrpIODOtxF7xvKoDKbSeu3MAXIVnPzPJ6OxczUEOydsrprTZC-iY3RmwTXvz-bmiGQ?key=rxGnIOzTXwvvF_Z1hOaPWA)
