## TTSZ
TTSZ is a rare forced dupe from Jigsaw, and can be also obtained from Grace, but it is possible to always avoid TTSZ from Grace System. Similar to JLOO, it has one good setup and is not very conducive to queue-based setups. Don’t be too scared by the very large solve count, it’s inflated by different boxes and SZ reductions.  
![](https://lh7-rt.googleusercontent.com/docsz/AD_4nXdRMLvDwhuCBuDO8awzmwd8aSP-siUwLcKmRYKazZ_06Uabta3z7sGOegUFjTga7uhuVcazKig1OJ5dP5o5e1Slkp3I1o5AChW20Kl61W7wi2ZyYhoP56qPpZ4i-6ui5wOL2SBdV7LtuYC4X7sQGUZLoMk?key=rxGnIOzTXwvvF_Z1hOaPWA)

## TTJL
TTJL is a forced dupe from a multitude of 1st setups, and is the embodiment of the idea of “sickly sweet” - something so sweet it tastes almost bitter. Too many TJL and most people just don’t know what to do. Approach it with some caution and you’ll be fine.  
![](https://lh7-rt.googleusercontent.com/docsz/AD_4nXfOnaWfXgy9esDij5qhqmv5ub2zNojzIgAgrms9aWHmeFSuojgTxG_gwHvHzfmnyqtvLtZBLFZFbmmLVO-yufhzUmxrIwKQrBXCdULJKptM7GDxhYegnOH_Tfu0xrEfyYgd5jtidTjm5gfMQv-Q8I3OhAgb?key=rxGnIOzTXwvvF_Z1hOaPWA)![](https://lh7-rt.googleusercontent.com/docsz/AD_4nXd2Omt9QJf24pjQ7MaJHXa1lCTWlXjHLla2md3VmfmRiOmqto1hR7tII56AAxteBCCjz9PMQ5f_W22Lo5oZa-M08k0Snik_f0eqCwP5A65--0iBwdKFqXhdVzlsh4wobmmnF1lwXXs-MxzHIc1MOdXzynhI?key=rxGnIOzTXwvvF_Z1hOaPWA)![](https://lh7-rt.googleusercontent.com/docsz/AD_4nXe7Wg3jRjavX-G3MhQitsGRJuNDvA6ob0YqLtuc5jsJuaPuDgXIE3MCd7vofItC2kx3vZv0smuq6psl6SB8An78Xs8j4uaaAYchcT1VYVp7t-gYcLnCP9MtxqHl46opEr5phJ-cCcqNzsunjNeS2985NibX?key=rxGnIOzTXwvvF_Z1hOaPWA)
![](https://lh7-rt.googleusercontent.com/docsz/AD_4nXfn5gg04E8IDISaFSdPvPa2SHGJfPSQRPRN80p66yVNK8EeTLcrhkvKqo__GCmagy7kS3jshQdnhHK9BE6ycuP6NBLuqScSX8dG1rQzcvC8E4gPb50j8gHRXUX6oHbJ6evqqcc3j_W2KHWBFVXkjiNQSZg?key=rxGnIOzTXwvvF_Z1hOaPWA)![](https://lh7-rt.googleusercontent.com/docsz/AD_4nXdaceXS1tdefvomC5J0agNELI28-1TKJ29ippCHl8QWxRZRSETTYmYM8jyB7NQ3Ub55IiV9aB0rnCnQUMOA9UhVtGks4JSAe66uNZrcgG-v4V9IiYKz--aT-23VLLJ-Tk-NJE0hPSBaeXyRW2aUg6C6Eum3?key=rxGnIOzTXwvvF_Z1hOaPWA)![](https://lh7-rt.googleusercontent.com/docsz/AD_4nXc2sH98Zl353PSjG0nLiVD13bJdBFowqw3KXiS5CcQ_j9T0uC4IOLZsCJ4FIYBDPPjgRSvrgNZtdD7_RHB8VdMn61Fh4m5f819GmdSxnjsegBWQ8J8SwBZ5ScijBnqdHRwxT-VVucrnEsvEdzTt01t6dnjA?key=rxGnIOzTXwvvF_Z1hOaPWA)  
You may recognize this from the IJLO-Z and IJLO-S queue-based setups. Abides by the same restrictions. For TLZ and TJS queues, you can take the fourth queue-based setup.
![](https://lh7-rt.googleusercontent.com/docsz/AD_4nXcjUxZ0tnIx_EKF_pBw_F5EO38_bGrMYX0kyOHY899yzQ2uSCDDEGQImOvkM-0hzuV_CfunhEUPqbGmCyOV0T8W-gK-lFqgi8yJySOHBoft0fihdT_DNKX_8EGzBw6pzX6yLsbGOem03999cYI1_Nwk1AF0?key=rxGnIOzTXwvvF_Z1hOaPWA)
This setup is for when you can access I generally, I before any two of JLT. In order, the solves are for  
1) S before J
2) J before S, L before S  
3) J before S, S before L  
![](https://lh7-rt.googleusercontent.com/docsz/AD_4nXdyQ9Q5pTADPAXOuzwnvVjR7AOJMAeiS8jZzNKS5UxcbRvWveCSHDZEpnE52IIwBemgo56NElBg-scZA7V7p8drpZ7cJ9O-P1asI900K7GvZX1Yqg1biMLJ8oavK6_ECxahnODMey4sFQtR9BECtu9qvL3B?key=rxGnIOzTXwvvF_Z1hOaPWA)![](https://lh7-rt.googleusercontent.com/docsz/AD_4nXcbQ0c2yD38nzRkAHGg_cpavBtffAULVsXce78KJVheggYrKhOINCWVKHCgP7XUT8_gefY6oFtTciX0k25H5addnaL0OYFNVdISAy-90HhESusQoKyhccS2sTOB7O-kej1vIqxW4toGNbok3r35C0ZYk--3?key=rxGnIOzTXwvvF_Z1hOaPWA)![](https://lh7-rt.googleusercontent.com/docsz/AD_4nXc0gEfN-rh5C7hTin2rsd49scJgi2I2KfZRNqgPTnc2nUVgwAcQcwSo4O_7cuuemFZZzbXsTTd1i-tFZO0I9qnSpQEn0Rzb6yWAC8jKhqe-ypB8ZG1ZbiiJ3P5asK1y5taxb_fZB01_i8HeQ0MjEp89rcyi?key=rxGnIOzTXwvvF_Z1hOaPWA)  
This setup is for when you see TL. In order, the solves are for  
1) S before J
2) J before S, Z before S  
3) J before S, S before Z  
![](https://lh7-rt.googleusercontent.com/docsz/AD_4nXfxgb9W78etCJElr98-Ugls9rA7I8yaQRPzKcZ0iSk8EIVfO2ONJ9b9rUHTEiF0yfqtt2KV3IuQffDm-f9ArxZCGE9K21kmL2mrW7NcvVx1MRElj1cdHwlVo0SdCKwllvJ-N2vYIN6k7LBR1CWMyjlM-Sfw?key=rxGnIOzTXwvvF_Z1hOaPWA)

![](https://lh7-rt.googleusercontent.com/docsz/AD_4nXfTbY_ZB0ha42dmSijos8PHyrUA_Nf0v1IWyVWTITnIwEeIIC-cUtBV5x4IS6HAlYbJO-BJgFNaogOwzDgEMjRJ_QsnmqdRCse93VZFKDA8-gYlbR0JITr1ytymlMSmuk9AGCRBDLUau0OJoRES2so2vM0?key=rxGnIOzTXwvvF_Z1hOaPWA)![](https://lh7-rt.googleusercontent.com/docsz/AD_4nXeRnzZ9FSHeadbUwAYGKHuZxRKsR9OrmfuMbiugYE3XCisDh8MpjK3L9lbWxFXTR6fHaap-lDWWLHc6FXCAKsBSI5I63ysNMV9YbO3GrALUHcV_2tMfdCIS0D9YM2a-GPvSIMr8345D6Q2VUTUsiQLCTSQo?key=rxGnIOzTXwvvF_Z1hOaPWA)![](https://lh7-rt.googleusercontent.com/docsz/AD_4nXfpowpRxo2MykksKIgpZWvwiaNfflsc9RM7OMz1aW7AEwoV4lFrKvcDRJYjXMqoIRHGJgAMTHdmV_PF9-VZ9unq-tQdt2DUS01ZigAl_UWMmPjw-wdjBLuRLn4TRD6wN5zUXX7SkwMO4eOpML9lkDWC8bUl?key=rxGnIOzTXwvvF_Z1hOaPWA)
Then, you’re left with JLO and IJL (specifically where JL is before I) queues. This setup works for see JL:  
![](https://lh7-rt.googleusercontent.com/docsz/AD_4nXdj7ZiTnWQUVSfOVW1xrITXSipjeCvOG8MPmwBppLJD91y1h6lT1pcX-XZ7n6LOvzN1ZJfLbws2KtEi4PIIAqqsYH6NMOL2E79BGZmrYfcGdKLQlwI8xoj1bRdf6EcskUE2VWThRwztehi1mwNcxgq4vU-F?key=rxGnIOzTXwvvF_Z1hOaPWA)

![](https://lh7-rt.googleusercontent.com/docsz/AD_4nXd01EXdiiS47CVgbeuFSWCcCNQbAPKxeIAv1oeN9-nStS7gPdMaJUJJEki5q7OKcN8O1L06IOFHjMlpgpqCGmRiCGHy_9EHhmsQshXZs6CgXPlMHHqJJn3TcHlZuNdAbXxDDcRUMzg5jdx0Uk7JheZQdRqP?key=rxGnIOzTXwvvF_Z1hOaPWA)![](https://lh7-rt.googleusercontent.com/docsz/AD_4nXfJzLltat3IATGiulLuMZt83iuVhbQaDv4KdYKHvk0Zo-wZERYeChESYm-R0PEoANNZze-DwuLemBwJSyr3e5A-8OgiS_sK7gjY9xCCiqHNczDOoK8ZKtu80k6296pdfpSk7h1qRcd4wbAK48zn7FA_8Z0?key=rxGnIOzTXwvvF_Z1hOaPWA)![](https://lh7-rt.googleusercontent.com/docsz/AD_4nXdpi2TCMkW8VXk3rcY7gffosjYOAAgk4IRNI_-PCFt_Q3qurVIQGoNYSh65dF6ADQNdLhiOcsq3kpdeSHHoR8qma6A2UXgGao7N8KldU3ab0xkMMxAHHQ0QcTLGrmIxE25LbjuffnaY9e-jOZZF8yHDyD8H?key=rxGnIOzTXwvvF_Z1hOaPWA)  
Z before SO, S before ZO, and O before SZ.
## TJJO/TLLO
TLLO is a forced dupe from Shoe + O. It has two one-piece queue-based setups, for S and Z. They’re similar to TJLO, but they actually prioritize saving T over O. One of them is entirely borrowed from TJOZ, and the second is the same setup as TJLO.
![](https://lh7-rt.googleusercontent.com/docsz/AD_4nXf3t6K85Zk_6LswJY2_wQlQxn8oV3gXOx0L_Ve1wmncV1xcoDPjfulnuKjm9NguvoDq8XbTSBHfE6FfI1qIZm7M7ypm27gGFwxVP8Whk2yfke68xBUJ2wR78AL2C6W4QOB4wLoGwmJCFeg6h8fCJh36xcg8?key=rxGnIOzTXwvvF_Z1hOaPWA)
![](https://lh7-rt.googleusercontent.com/docsz/AD_4nXdM6RxyD-n8FIZJAX7aTEjphFWatsZo2xNP_ELrOiVKeNEI2_Hq1I-d-YZ8-IEbmYDAwQksQMxZneeo8afR0mN5oHDFN76J5lflgJWz1HJRS8goMVnPT1FiihXx6XTewQBj7JOV_QNHqAQ6Nw0BK-UqakSS?key=rxGnIOzTXwvvF_Z1hOaPWA)![](https://lh7-rt.googleusercontent.com/docsz/AD_4nXcjttt1mv26vwKSk8pK0-_h9va9EOkxX28N84XwUiGYW64ZzctBXks9uJLiKFNwv2Tkf-quwGGq9gbr4qVMtMdsgUCIvyZjeEw95LHiYI8hnmoNt-1X7boGFte6hV0rUJkizDcUELCV_qyRv0--shvP7mMn?key=rxGnIOzTXwvvF_Z1hOaPWA)![](https://lh7-rt.googleusercontent.com/docsz/AD_4nXfthmxyLlZmFP8NGg-we2S_V08kpMq0NhVM7f_TQ64zXrIbzjzsnu9hbChTk022Jx0tHCsZaGaQlkhpwoHFjGUPjW9XlsrYFD-sOZzb1panyy_k0pihk70i3wydR0yAyXT7f5dT_p_3pn7lpL-2S0JzG9j1?key=rxGnIOzTXwvvF_Z1hOaPWA)![](https://lh7-rt.googleusercontent.com/docsz/AD_4nXf0sGLM5qyLm998gZBmTerhHYlCTXbGWQRHaMQzf5j0Bu45eZ3U9ezfF31UtQ6urL-iUDRhAnKORxY_JiLcrB2RHwyUDV2uFIHkP5eNINqLrA04H1iK0tbdjLIfAWX4VbWCSzsMpjrM8CUNjps9HhdBECmM?key=rxGnIOzTXwvvF_Z1hOaPWA)
This is the see S setup, entirely borrowed from TJOZ. Same rules.

![](https://lh7-rt.googleusercontent.com/docsz/AD_4nXeR_cpdfnp7qyPnuBI98ZJ4XqOyWoULUDFsuXD8NEGRx-cE1KrCZt3XbXKK_2tLFN5Y7LuV3fjkPgunVse_yAo3FfNL85colshHUDw_mKoooxM8n6A6sB1U4fPOXTeaDmDrXyau1lHdjOuBeYQsreFqQwg?key=rxGnIOzTXwvvF_Z1hOaPWA)![](https://lh7-rt.googleusercontent.com/docsz/AD_4nXeKImXHzJfPCdf1vUUJlnJoNFfKWPr4oAyyShcoru0x9UAEtLLRaXPuWbNmMWNF7As_6wtvuxE8WpMBFk0Atrz1vDrTqdC4mxRQO3R1w_7W0ZpHMatadvNBJoHlFzww2tqOvjYvpnEo41fYBVgGFl0oANLg?key=rxGnIOzTXwvvF_Z1hOaPWA)![](https://lh7-rt.googleusercontent.com/docsz/AD_4nXdUY4dmj09h5jmgsG3duxl3Z9wD5fdvYvFp2v7xX8CoUXSutIU-GMrEi8xZH_zKoLm0Fha-QUxdgWAGESbAB8O2wYD6gTjbPF7lKg41OSX3Xh9haYGnjvUib3RIY7NwhmxuH8pO8m-Et-b1kz2Hr9pn0Cc?key=rxGnIOzTXwvvF_Z1hOaPWA)![](https://lh7-rt.googleusercontent.com/docsz/AD_4nXdrKbPks_JNlZ9pSU4d8xZ90xlZC9umS38FKAaYd4lSbHXyGHXKCfQVrVJTEINoq7YXKiS7xDKxoIm6OrXgb91nkCxduI7gKE8Z2Wrl3mh9QSexqW158dgfYDq1YzEh5AmsfqE3mopo_kVWnbKUl1AnkFTL?key=rxGnIOzTXwvvF_Z1hOaPWA)
This is the see Z setup. Because every solve has a Z before S dependency, you should use this after the see S setup. It also doesn’t have 100% save O/T on\[TIZ]! queues, where the see TI setup can be used.

Then, if you see either LJ or JO, this setup will be 100% O/T.
![](https://lh7-rt.googleusercontent.com/docsz/AD_4nXcLijbGB5NttGC6KM0_Fk_Jc9MGFQ6-sQCXR7iOezx01BGJBFkkKrfjkoSy5PiXO6X8kjl4VdAD9hnL1odtVpdUJqFNY61Xry-YISfR5kgs7dwIWEuntUO9I1ZOJ62WHY7xl6Rzs2iMWryNCbqQONMsqLvn?key=rxGnIOzTXwvvF_Z1hOaPWA)  
![](https://lh7-rt.googleusercontent.com/docsz/AD_4nXe-iTJRqSH58uMI98fvsVL6HSthPy81hhrX42z4Z1VQCC3kx_A8TNSiDnfhx3U26BbCyc8O2kGsWg-VN2rR6YwUIlxVM0Y4mfGzfRh8s-1u0CBHJ33gW18HrzrVFWbHxqNf-pBm9vYexDsvVf6vCvPenzJq?key=rxGnIOzTXwvvF_Z1hOaPWA)![](https://lh7-rt.googleusercontent.com/docsz/AD_4nXegD3TGTz5KMQjNBPzQAq8om5pfvXJ00Gml1MK_m617SL_IEdkAhpt_PEMVVAL4Z3-LAsU7Wfu94yDslsXyZJzFvXunxCnJ-ONJF6QFh8ddqHrvHUIkKSYaqeTsZ1dwVXnJtu3AIM8MMVSH9uItiNKkDS3m?key=rxGnIOzTXwvvF_Z1hOaPWA)![](https://lh7-rt.googleusercontent.com/docsz/AD_4nXcaroFXEDxasp9mwMs5UqdMxLHs0bhMTmX7-C2gMi29S4N2XL2JKfDwX_idQjRpLao_niQQkWOmP2n9wx6CNP_L9ygtniqgqtz-9WblHJH9RfQWC7I1uFW75etCtsvBOI89uez669Z69LBWVwdzR8RKfAoG?key=rxGnIOzTXwvvF_Z1hOaPWA)![](https://lh7-rt.googleusercontent.com/docsz/AD_4nXcg7pGblWGsmQS5mRj-H9FzcRYTFVPJUpi0Bh6Y8dnNGXGokkF-z0aWT3NWrcz7wTFjtPyUjjyCKk3QZx2mge74QHmVy4AZTVVTdJjPAomXlHzehugZz3u0acat4XHFHl8cK3X2WPhigglVCoTOWtDzBvxt?key=rxGnIOzTXwvvF_Z1hOaPWA)
These four solves are broken into two sets of two queues to read: O before I (first half), or TI before O (second half) and then after that, it’s broken into SZ order
![](https://lh7-rt.googleusercontent.com/docsz/AD_4nXeg-0DAk8li-wxZh1ug-mpdeODG7w8hF2NxcjJHVy-nEfQeEWl-HGrHYsRilqZ1JbZ6wL2MMxCao763NzEHpDm0G6BLa_I-3S5kAWT3EYpYrYxWb7uZntEwxdA2vKVupFSBVILST56_z7iLlKhqzy4tn4s?key=rxGnIOzTXwvvF_Z1hOaPWA)![](https://lh7-rt.googleusercontent.com/docsz/AD_4nXdtSATkpEKICaaAHhVv6tXpbEMJVJqiUqFVdPV5Oo79U2pxyqwtUuyXsvs7nfcx92_iyXJ1C5sWadPZNG4KJ_7LaZmsgV6r2JUKmhh8XK0yr14Hj6iRjpELvbMgmHBPtTXzh1ZNKfenyO-Kt4zPF2Y_Nf8?key=rxGnIOzTXwvvF_Z1hOaPWA)
The two JO solves are almost the exact same as two of the LJ solves. Never place the L to fill the box first, and 180 the J in the first solve if necessary.

Then, if you see ILO, there’s a necessary 3-piece setup. Sadly, I don’t think there’s something better.

![](https://lh7-rt.googleusercontent.com/docsz/AD_4nXfwD4uorxdSmXZShDgRwGVJrDjMe41OuFNMQWT-ds_zxtCN-3QAaUCxoB_IEdmF9aVTQvCU0-eS-kqaegCj23q9gQ625LeQnlXwDSxOGTuvWti4-F9DnBUnld8UQ30iq4COWJH2siVtj2pyHqoDEddZEWbk?key=rxGnIOzTXwvvF_Z1hOaPWA)
![](https://lh7-rt.googleusercontent.com/docsz/AD_4nXfVRRNWB4VRla2xE6qPKwVmOSli-BTR3_G_k8cf7SNdYQgKIpau0708rYHj6PaiVH34q0YNn0ctIx4flA51tXgbFEsCOEOru3MdhUU56ECkWiK5hPIjAX6jYGcZScGzc0S9iONWJe6oiKh6jPrbHscF8fM?key=rxGnIOzTXwvvF_Z1hOaPWA)![](https://lh7-rt.googleusercontent.com/docsz/AD_4nXcfkI8GMSxm2AJKbQKc9qaP-2tmOW09nJILHAqlB8GHPeqqcMK-hXO40wZnHOa0RCCdEK1idMSxDYrKFCjMBHeHbBWiAKDp_A3C92sii52WMEMVvHsp5AC4pH9vAZGrqrjZc3iObHPyqsfysO8yjsX5PeGF?key=rxGnIOzTXwvvF_Z1hOaPWA)![](https://lh7-rt.googleusercontent.com/docsz/AD_4nXelwWOJWVTErklPkWIUTcTICtys70_p15WtgkuKuciBUMwv1rMMRVNn4qwd9Ys7pEsvcmCZJoHmE742k4v8zTPvPXjn2B2tAyPzdf330m2mx5-LM3ree7ytwtqZ0fgoz0SQJ6uQUekUXIClcg_5W1uXdhKE?key=rxGnIOzTXwvvF_Z1hOaPWA)  
Solves are for S before Z, S last, and then Z before S before J, when the first two solves don’t work.
![](https://lh7-rt.googleusercontent.com/docsz/AD_4nXdjbSCaddtKXn-4JUfHbh7Ns2UgsHyffHRg7LfgFbuE0t_Wv8IZp2j6g0T-B_4ObkRuoVVRWgVmVkb5tbG7SuJ2nw34KTEy62cz0Do6lJ99eUMwC8IXrNSe0erWLfaYHYcTarveQ-twuUe-u19t-fQCEud7?key=rxGnIOzTXwvvF_Z1hOaPWA)
![](https://lh7-rt.googleusercontent.com/docsz/AD_4nXdVTG7Vxx175vwqrLL7H2NPStoE69GX_rUSBhu5pCjEsHXoFD_29R2ZY3pbIztKl7UGuKFufdfUbPp7EIjJEIbTxtndqzAIwEdb_fXZQIS-WPW6q_3gBpowi27LG-vXuSpjajAYBQNQuxzcz9FS4Q3PKPs?key=rxGnIOzTXwvvF_Z1hOaPWA)![](https://lh7-rt.googleusercontent.com/docsz/AD_4nXesbmLAvWq0FPETuFXNj5yn725-lZqz_cUiCTQJ2WoOO07v7thDHWpjf0nzV6fPFpqn_N0okb3rSlnhfQUH8Wc9HSBXFWaBumxGA9LgYzuR0RsvxyMWmTadsiAk5XxSdYA948kQkTqGZ6wslBZEo3zwhYvj?key=rxGnIOzTXwvvF_Z1hOaPWA)
This is for when you see TL. Unfortunately, it’s another 3-piece setup. First solve is for I, J, or S last (S last needs 180) and the second solve is for Z last.

Lastly, you have two options for when you see TIO. I’ve chosen the one I like the most. 
![](https://lh7-rt.googleusercontent.com/docsz/AD_4nXeu0ohiVwb_v-GincAEGk1DQdV86193CxY4H_L7Ww9DDhHRvhq06czMrsEfIpmYmoWO8qxAXo1kgjnNPRTHaOpiqoTdGb_aPMgnCvUksxltHUpmClJtNkGCuiq9UKoGWW1pnLY_ejyji89INQDPK5wuAFoe?key=rxGnIOzTXwvvF_Z1hOaPWA)
![](https://lh7-rt.googleusercontent.com/docsz/AD_4nXf4CJVdA3w0zLbh3SAcZKJUWBkNynvS9RGs4ajOHRb0DCaLoYZdcIdVxI4zPqPEiztRZ6_ErtXV3UE5jD-4TwnaXxO1McxGiMfscrKyc2QykmnjKQYcG1apJgR6JsqCYQvM13oVFqi3Bjem57jxWFr5-74Z?key=rxGnIOzTXwvvF_Z1hOaPWA)![](https://lh7-rt.googleusercontent.com/docsz/AD_4nXdW2v6wRAxp9nTg9OuOd7hksQht8F4EFVjWiXKcm7O7-P30AvpkRZo4aYRORYBMQ8HgM9txP7OZfOod1eBO_qDZva87gf2X74_idrbUIvi90X7VXoU0aJeXrwRLyiP8P1djuxRuX4mYkqqIKDQw3x3Lf1jB?key=rxGnIOzTXwvvF_Z1hOaPWA)![](https://lh7-rt.googleusercontent.com/docsz/AD_4nXdIaH2IzyKx1CEuCTGX2pR0GF7iZi1B6SRUJ_yA51dZyCd7W6GnfhvvKUfi0FwLX3nmC_XLSs_DfWvOXq9TW3TVfgK5xVQH-oT2LBvGAC2YDsgKHocIVzMAv7DAJGBIV7dwN3OqgQSAkGCuPdCcBbi5hTQ?key=rxGnIOzTXwvvF_Z1hOaPWA)
![](https://lh7-rt.googleusercontent.com/docsz/AD_4nXcx8dQhXNpE9Nc4a_jSEkOWcjifAi4V6lg38p9D0sHoy_lCufKh9SF3Tdz8RxnPeHGvT5ut7MPWFdjhNLZ2zN3ibVJu2Q7TorY8t4gjqXG1O0IxT36ZFXOtqZJ6_-uoscP7hU9YV9zgmzYhwSLbM5pg-oOX?key=rxGnIOzTXwvvF_Z1hOaPWA)![](https://lh7-rt.googleusercontent.com/docsz/AD_4nXc9VbkkUgXEcoeHRWfL_7n8cci27vMP7vQw10szCC2LqJs4WvLXydRk7fN2k9ME4yDWvXJytL5E-O4mpUfIGGL4lzPv60LYRKLFFqoWX5EXc6uRBiYBLx0aGmwlz-4K3vU0ZURondmHJNvVYCr4KqTAItNS?key=rxGnIOzTXwvvF_Z1hOaPWA)
The first three solves are for S, Z, and L last, respectively. The last two are for J last: not L<S<Z and L<S<Z.
## TJJL/TJLL
TJJL is a forced dupe from PCO + I and PCO + O setups. It only needs four solves for 100% O, and will look nigh-identical to IJLO’s 100% T method.  
TJ will always be placed here. You don’t need to place them, but it’s useful to know that those placements are guaranteed
![](https://lh7-rt.googleusercontent.com/docsz/AD_4nXd9A-Je6Dj9FgqUBmG4iZ1LfPsyaqoW_3gYETGtSggz5-MUUnqs2q0xzYMuw9FPAAuSlH6ZzWfUQ9h7P5mTWjWoLKjp6LFtQlL_eGJvsGRDYhsEQiULnimiBHRi1D4NNEUbBmjP-Fvp0Nlnc_O1-P7HDkRU?key=rxGnIOzTXwvvF_Z1hOaPWA)  
If you see S before Z or J before L, place L. If you see the opposite (Z<S or L<J), place J.
![](https://lh7-rt.googleusercontent.com/docsz/AD_4nXePpyY6jWOx9HzwvLnAfEcOIK0UEqxhEC7RF3tHg4Rmy5uXrTk_VZKZbsWfSnp2cjbVM_VgTGh5sCJewrUKwrqshXHUrBEhHqk_g0gDvuXU2UWAGkgNHcYFGylgmRv824OLxKKbka2OlmV11RgOV3kVFbUv?key=rxGnIOzTXwvvF_Z1hOaPWA)![](https://lh7-rt.googleusercontent.com/docsz/AD_4nXcku3-eXkZCXGCRqlvGWSsEtlPs7kMQEPcLDsejOgwvV0qzp-sCVzswbf4RSM0iduniHngBfMOUr5igEM6Dby75-nlV8SZbZykY5_oVgQFrB_vgl70XlU4bxlyHrzoNBx8JJEZ5zRbfOsIWWgSyXqR45ZM?key=rxGnIOzTXwvvF_Z1hOaPWA)

## TJJZ/TLLS
TJJZ is a forced dupe from IJOZ Hill setup. It is also one of two odd-T 2nds to be 100% T.  
It has three single-piece queue-based setups, for L and S/Z

![](https://lh7-rt.googleusercontent.com/docsz/AD_4nXeU1Rg795Lv4abqe3tvlMsbQlDemu3DqxW67JrVbdXV9ZulVop-VjwRVCOzEKANPehA9vz9I-vaNpBJ1wjvLEvsCGfIMtUNdRZbTjfrQ__UivuGzZ64eEZqVibZEQRKmxybbfkiv_hLdCkpY_nTkmJ5IAD2?key=rxGnIOzTXwvvF_Z1hOaPWA)![](https://lh7-rt.googleusercontent.com/docsz/AD_4nXew7SQGyUnqXQo329JRK9J056Yu6f5C5xHDOrI5KFcPLOOaPZou3PoM_SQ8BVx3m6jhXKGH_j2mdAnH7-rers2I7QM2SfO74D2RyvWoS7H1ia8l-e6eRscJ-1c_WUmF94M356hrIGMbzFxslLUz-pZ7XrlX?key=rxGnIOzTXwvvF_Z1hOaPWA)![](https://lh7-rt.googleusercontent.com/docsz/AD_4nXeYrpuDFlEysE1aLDnrlOIO1zVHs2F6G10UwKKefE9JjENfzn-eNKonkwEhbwCKQDEmI-zLqdikijr9AgMKGbNeKbHzvmKg4eqtkKRbYOsK4mmRk_sxyHCB6o0-gst0lYu0kk-AYgLq78ngT4HtHwn8_Dr6?key=rxGnIOzTXwvvF_Z1hOaPWA)

See L queuebased setup. Fails on\[IO]!L queues.  
![](https://lh7-rt.googleusercontent.com/docsz/AD_4nXcpvginmyLnfm4u0x5CI9aqtIgWZx6EEJB4MqRHKN7DpR3Wz9CXKMDHUg4vEjs3eBSA9Z-IHITo_PMqOoaRngCIL4C1sMT-BtWIpJwKG0bnKwlbI2Iny_IqrXMpxcqbALwRPUWaFy0UAML8Pzy_F7ykuMYV?key=rxGnIOzTXwvvF_Z1hOaPWA)

This is the see S or Z queue-based setup. Fails on various queues with SO or ZT in them. The first row is the queue reading for see S, the second is for see Z.

ILO queue-based setup. It’s a congruent to TSSZ’s ILO queue-based setup, actually.

TZO uses the first and second solve. TJO uses the first solve. IJO uses every solve.
## TTIS/TTIZ
TTIS is a forced dupe from the LOSZ partial of 5p Jaws. It has multiple single-piece queue-based setups, but only a few are always buildable.  
![](https://lh7-rt.googleusercontent.com/docsz/AD_4nXfO_JXZvnrkc8Rq0flz1fMY4JJJNFy2onYntGHTYGc2VwVrzoNsIO6TY5KvIkVFlEUgbw1GCqclTwt73lgAv26rXvTxRNDR9onmc_xB4dxZXqRSmpmdoLxQRXwAJd5Wm9RUaI1Em1sAumfP6FebnfpD5DXx?key=rxGnIOzTXwvvF_Z1hOaPWA)

This is the S before J queue-based setup. First two solves are for I/T last, where it is based on OL order. Last solve is L/O last. This fails on TJS queues, where a TJ queue-based setup can be used.

This is the respective counterpart for see Z. You’ll have to use an LZ queue-based setup for this, though.

## TTIO
TTIO is a forced dupe from IJOZ Cliff setup. It is one out of two known 2nds to be forced into OQB for 100% T/O chance.  
TTIO has a see S and see Z save T queue-based setup.  
![](https://lh7-rt.googleusercontent.com/docsz/AD_4nXc7TUW0ITqLlSXnJeLxo4YlVMplHNyxGdgHJL2qw_nvQ_yfebHxDJKFnE6cvaQBY984ougqB7XYuKzsuTHCKqbZR-DkLaVSoULLaHsiTTv1hyRQKwnT7kw2S3QI0gtFhY-EUS0iGECx6MCXPdZFYZUTGPv5?key=rxGnIOzTXwvvF_Z1hOaPWA)![](https://lh7-rt.googleusercontent.com/docsz/AD_4nXdErYbm0O8O6OuCc34Uf49HqsaT6Xn7rRTQAzh5e3PpRkXbRvtDuJehom8EdES_zvCvfdjwdDKQEScQdJK6682BBkE--Xos1aYshgrduSd0_uRRc3-G0XwQB2M6a6-jNSkP45feeMRvBtKghbGydPRtUUGD?key=rxGnIOzTXwvvF_Z1hOaPWA)![](https://lh7-rt.googleusercontent.com/docsz/AD_4nXcvKq7os3eXof3I7azURZrNQhBxKTvaNatK0gvrM7pZFsgCUiO46-HbiGpmfo7Ha30lvvPf1o77nM6fu2_4XBHEYOmDQkYC6-XDrZBq1zl1R5ncvVVkiQX1Ikm2-xMtz3yR8HzMxaLIHbny5zfK8-Um5w?key=rxGnIOzTXwvvF_Z1hOaPWA)

![](https://lh7-rt.googleusercontent.com/docsz/AD_4nXcrv9_GcQQy80RjUzUoXmpbfRwmBkwcDsafUDE2DSukbzNRmjrVXkARlNx2WTve24WSDUGzWPT-lpjZaG0pxxutzyxAIB_WWRnKlyCYiKF5ZYH_jQsiNmiehBiif7kFJEa6YU9zxmIDYvO3YRmf_v5Rir-I?key=rxGnIOzTXwvvF_Z1hOaPWA)![](https://lh7-rt.googleusercontent.com/docsz/AD_4nXeXeHL1zxqEZRYZvr8SFsspavYjwhb4c-1vCm2Sjmd8F6h6ZOQNjxfVlKefcccUT7xdKOvRaz6L8w4mD0DMl2UJspEvRf3S9csH7yl9zAXRfcgbs_M6fvGzvSTPedLxfH6WX6pQ7xJv2dLUvfbvrSmmIikC?key=rxGnIOzTXwvvF_Z1hOaPWA)![](https://lh7-rt.googleusercontent.com/docsz/AD_4nXfoHEajPU_vyI7X-VrClCu0MZVr3WdZ6s3KU_HY0DTM1X4yPTrTZQaRO3hyse-iavnR2mv7La5NTWQQSJ5He1qKrwcpccNQZGkEHxEjKv6jrll-ger-6Vn_MaWdiQfKrYqvUcSjtsq3kbrx1G6q7PePvBQ?key=rxGnIOzTXwvvF_Z1hOaPWA)

Solves are based on JO/LO order. They fail when any two of ITL is before S, where either the IS queue-based setup works, or the L/J queue-based setup works.

These are the IS and IZ queue-based setups. Directly after this point, which is see TIO, TTIO suffers the worst difficulty spike seen in PC anywhere in my opinion. There are no always-buildable 100% T/O 3ps for all\[TIO]! queues (although, one does exist for one where you can access T in the next bag of\[TIO]!) and there is only one usable 3-piece for 100% T/I saving.  

This will be the first and only time I will permit using OQB to simplify saves. This is because I genuinely believe it to be better.  
![](https://lh7-rt.googleusercontent.com/docsz/AD_4nXcUL7f0RbWUUSIupydP4E-96jd2dU9-x2iNNHOKG_I6jW0FlDMe-p-J1asqhEjiquJnkCFNCrTwkf-B7c98fc6yZq44TiF4V44Da_B-VfyZvjNTrvP7qPEhmiSqaS2NL9xhVBHt4TRTVhVeQvjZtkvc4L0?key=rxGnIOzTXwvvF_Z1hOaPWA)

Queue reading is based on which piece comes next after the J you revealed: S, Z, and L respectively.
## X-JLSS/JLZZ
JLSS is a forced dupe from the LZ Hill + Heart setup.  
![](https://lh7-rt.googleusercontent.com/docsz/AD_4nXe1325ZibVmqBdCpSQHRwbdMTBrfaMb9bf99bODGgljxv3rzPx3xh9DPoBpXqc2y8XKbZ9yqVn7OmaDHkUbh90M8WB2b7UveoJvFHNezHmlDToxENiTQdirnb1eRa70Vo88mtYEwQnZCPqPoSTPSPPYCdrx?key=rxGnIOzTXwvvF_Z1hOaPWA)![](https://lh7-rt.googleusercontent.com/docsz/AD_4nXcWoH5Q-SoDndachuS3j-T9RcMfMQrFPzhB7CJTzx_15kKs0GhlNi9_3xsLuEeNJ1kP-RrE5t6NX4FtrrJPU60LUFa3JLhO4vvDjgnEFyYh7aMLhNr6xbJEULmNEet92GFSY0qQFHaV0_2pWTFl7S6xDkeD?key=rxGnIOzTXwvvF_Z1hOaPWA)![](https://lh7-rt.googleusercontent.com/docsz/AD_4nXcj7oTczYp6agAFoO9Ldkt_gA05Fsfrndv8G7H-kTY2sU8W7aRqF--F5Yjp01xDuyZPvm0FOK40sR61gckCVdjv5m91kwsZXRcS6xjV7BAR4igakfOgedfAD_D8_OGwosCw2pvM71WpmChz01xOFjv19R18?key=rxGnIOzTXwvvF_Z1hOaPWA)  
Surprisingly, the see S queue-based setup is much easier than the see Z queue-based setup. This fails on queues where any two of\[LZO] are before S. All queues except LOS will be able to use the Z queue-based setup, where the LO queue-based setup can be used then.

![](https://lh7-rt.googleusercontent.com/docsz/AD_4nXeax8BbFmxZ6N6bZl07lUBC8Saml_082vrVeD3leRKPF-MDSieZBBRWC--jvWLcstKPaRm5vSqsaaGhr9HWdgyZvabLA5ktHDg45mWKBKnayWq-GCHpjYjI5hXJzYv7iqCBtD4qwA8PTnHcxEKJYRKslmY?key=rxGnIOzTXwvvF_Z1hOaPWA)
![](https://lh7-rt.googleusercontent.com/docsz/AD_4nXfdVjhjA-nBiQEVQQrfKfy9ukcn-6tSBI9mfEmFTuce9vguYy_IVCiojhJVFL7Xp9IBKuoXrzOgnFK-iwWuRcMg4giSq1Q25VXiiuyOf_hPhpD3o5WnGQRQZJ-fYWMzmEb4w0XGv6Ewmj-8P_Ki58J_Wjkm?key=rxGnIOzTXwvvF_Z1hOaPWA)![](https://lh7-rt.googleusercontent.com/docsz/AD_4nXdqCAuhdJ9-fDiPoMsoRLE4N4pfGVGZllsAH8-wSjtJRTKKaFwiSwGxUXuDEusQc_8o7Zua9PVUQfcy4IUF89OrqRCPAYVmTO-lDQNP99LIaBfE0CICVA2gLUX6Z-cGN5IlW2EsXx8JXPGwPq7a-p0OM-td?key=rxGnIOzTXwvvF_Z1hOaPWA)![](https://lh7-rt.googleusercontent.com/docsz/AD_4nXc1Z480-qFwdWR1bg_r_SMqFBH9HjktcOAurPTXK-AZkveQZGz5SZchqiVqZ-O_6xlQ3UFJdgkPxxgfdYqAOeGbxkv9Vk3e4xqiYqOu-qrXHzA1CUpJ5ns8dw-x0jDiCdtxiX551NiPbbYtYqeRdh_Pm5sG?key=rxGnIOzTXwvvF_Z1hOaPWA)  
These are the first three solves of the see Z queue-based setup. In order, they are for T/I last, J/O last, then L last. If J is last, and you saw\[TO]!Z as the queue, you will actually have to use the second solve in the next set. The next three are specifically for S last. 

![](https://lh7-rt.googleusercontent.com/docsz/AD_4nXeqadlp87VRhTBBR-Zg0p8VIFw5MYriMdZ4e-iXT2mHCrJ6mttuBOQZDaGC3nO5qvmYUrmR03O1lghOQLhUgBqSyU25ecIkCRvOiLm0h3C4qZ0n3THsqSJ887HiLYUnZpFAKZvjbArsRptU8t92KHQGusk?key=rxGnIOzTXwvvF_Z1hOaPWA)![](https://lh7-rt.googleusercontent.com/docsz/AD_4nXe2yJx8Zp-VEHSmWKeKizg1LGVSXifRrlWCOvdZFTzT3i4LETDUZTUZ42DS69kMsdga_3mmqRK292RgLc3Gu2ydiFKhH0HUG72c6NMXYjY_ZC-JYWnoGLjNLXnyBCqG-Tni5BjWzqcoe3JPo_1KDRDcmxwE?key=rxGnIOzTXwvvF_Z1hOaPWA)![](https://lh7-rt.googleusercontent.com/docsz/AD_4nXe3X2tCslP1Js2HLlZJKlR84KYA1tJYt1WszrLXk5bTHtDNH3Z0mU8R1EDgRDLUY8EsIK_KUoq_3C52Wp1KbYhPJcr9zX_WDoeji0oiXoveScqFzsuRJ9VLyp4hTeDnjLT0jC0RZOuKytJHCNpnXpddLrAz?key=rxGnIOzTXwvvF_Z1hOaPWA)
For S last queues, don’t place the S on the bottom first, that’s where it should be placed last.  
  ## X-TOSS/TOZZ
TOSS is a forced dupe from the IJLS partial Jigsaw setup
## TJOO/TLOO
TJOO is a forced dupe from IJLS box. Dupe O and no I piece doesn’t give very many options for queue-based setups, so there’s the PCO+O 100% O/T setup.

## TIOO
TIOO is a forced dupe from IJLS box. The general 3p is 99.72% O/T, and mirroring it takes care of most of the solve fail queues, except\[TJL]! queues. The listed 3p will be specifically for when you see L before J or no LJ.

![](https://lh7-rt.googleusercontent.com/docsz/AD_4nXe4Ki-ZGtC98NTGkAJoeQxHpetiL_YMztFsYvtl0z2fcVVCyyTIIdgTsNSlQZ3aHIsgLRY0SMQhy1IftyV3yQzLSNLbwkiIyR9ORJNPZ7cPPLHZOxabqrDBsbsMAdMbIpZlGK2yJi8tUHAMQB0R2hxOM4dY?key=rxGnIOzTXwvvF_Z1hOaPWA)![](https://lh7-rt.googleusercontent.com/docsz/AD_4nXcuyofHEkeQykH5OWvH0PJvFQIFFI3lna5vK6ZC91vkc4zSjpf4MD0rYoh-j4IyfV78lDVoRXC1ngW4TOFeh9S8VdWyRKJBnleG8UdtBAqLhwoX6BzgSc8eYnHg_LFWwVVk7lUqyiMxmF3DYi8ab0LBg0g?key=rxGnIOzTXwvvF_Z1hOaPWA)![](https://lh7-rt.googleusercontent.com/docsz/AD_4nXeZauSUi6QrMtpZwFXoVm_OK_ncfggqk7ty0E6SqsK2XmXjXA39gXEDNlulretpejCcb6bhqG9n7PVtHGYqs4rYBjW-kajcSLUsne3z5WBRoSVhDuAYlbymYuJUG0jrdykWHTiwGCSQ7uS30S2wWN3QUY5J?key=rxGnIOzTXwvvF_Z1hOaPWA)
